### [1] [On Periodic Geodesics of Half-Lie Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26843)
*Martin Bauer,Levin Maier*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Hilbert半Lie群上强右不变黎曼度量的周期测地线存在性，证明了在非平凡基本群下每个自由同伦类存在周期测地线，并建立了Lyusternik-Fet型定理。在高阶同伦群非平凡且满足Palais-Smale条件时，证明了非平凡可缩周期测地线的存在性。结果推广至Sobolev微分同胚群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解无限维黎曼几何中哪些经典有限维原理仍然成立，特别是关于周期测地线的存在性。

Method: 利用Hilbert半Lie群的完备性结果，结合同伦理论、Palais-Smale条件（模右平移），以及紧致有限维全测地子流形的约化原理。

Result: (1) 非平凡基本群下，每个非平凡自由同伦类存在周期测地线；(2) 建立了Lyusternik-Fet型定理；(3) 高阶同伦群非平凡时，存在非平凡可缩周期测地线；(4) 结果可应用于Sobolev微分同胚群的右不变Sobolev度量。

Conclusion: 无限维情形下，第一和更高阶同伦信息仍然能强制周期测地线的存在性，与有限维经典结论相呼应。

Abstract: A central program in infinite-dimensional Riemannian geometry is to understand which classical finite-dimensional principles remain valid beyond finite dimensions. In this article, we study the existence of periodic geodesics on Hilbert half-Lie groups equipped with strong right-invariant Riemannian metrics. Building on recently established completeness results for this class of infinite-dimensional manifolds, we prove that every nontrivial free homotopy class contains a periodic geodesic whenever the fundamental group is nontrivial. We further establish a Lyusternik-Fet type theorem in this setting. Assuming a Palais-Smale condition modulo right translations and the existence of a nontrivial higher homotopy group, we prove the existence of a nonconstant contractible periodic geodesic. Thus, as in the finite-dimensional setting, both first and higher homotopy information continue to force the existence of periodic geodesics in infinite dimensions. In addition, we describe a reduction principle based on compact finite-dimensional totally geodesic submanifolds and apply our results to groups of Sobolev diffeomorphisms equipped with right-invariant Sobolev metrics.

</details>


### [2] [On triviality and scalar curvature estimation of gradient h-almost Yamabe solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26113)
*Absos Ali Shaikh,Ananya Tripathi*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了梯度h-几乎Yamabe孤立子在紧致及完备非紧致黎曼流形上的性质，通过标量曲率与孤立子函数的积分不等式建立了平凡性条件，获得了标量曲率估计，推广和细化了前人的研究成果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索梯度h-几乎Yamabe孤立子在紧致与非紧致黎曼流形上的平凡性条件，推广并细化已有的几乎Yamabe孤立子和h-几乎Yamabe孤立子的结论。

Method: 利用涉及标量曲率和孤立子函数的积分不等式，结合L²可积条件及函数h的符号分析，建立孤立子平凡性的充分条件，并推导标量曲率的估计。

Result: 获得了若干关于梯度h-几乎Yamabe孤立子平凡性的充分条件，给出了在特定L²可积条件下的标量曲率估计，并明确了函数h的符号作用。

Conclusion: 本文的结果推广并细化了关于几乎Yamabe孤立子和h-几乎Yamabe孤立子的现有工作，刻画了广义Yamabe孤立子的几何结构。

Abstract: In this study we have explored gradient $h$-almost Yamabe solitons on both compact and complete non-compact Riemannian manifolds. We have established several sufficient conditions for the triviality of such solitons with respect to integral inequalities involving the scalar curvature and the soliton function. In this regard, we have acquired scalar curvature estimation under certain $L^2$-integrability conditions, and defined signal of the function $h$. Our results extend and refine former works on almost and $h$-almost Yamabe solitons, and characterize the geometric structures of generalized Yamabe solitons.

</details>


### [3] [Godbillon-Vey classes of Lie subalgebroids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27340)
*Shuhei Yonehara*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文通过李代数胚框架，为奇异叶状结构定义了Godbillon-Vey类，研究了其性质并给出了若干例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Godbillon-Vey类是正则叶状结构的重要次级示性类，但将其推广到奇异叶状结构一直存在困难，尚未有完整结果。

Method: 固定一个李代数胚，在其李子代数胚上相对地定义Godbillon-Vey类，并研究其性质。

Result: 成功地在李代数胚框架下为奇异叶状结构定义了Godbillon-Vey类，并展示了若干具体例子。

Conclusion: 该工作为奇异叶状结构的Godbillon-Vey类研究提供了新的有效途径。

Abstract: The Godbillon-Vey class is a secondary characteristic class which is defined for regular foliations and have been studied extensively. On the other hand, extending the Godbillon-Vey class to singular foliations is difficult, and a complete result has not yet been obtained. In this paper, we address this problem by focusing on a geometric object called a Lie algebroid on a manifold. More precisely, we fix a Lie algebroid and relatively define the Godbillon-Vey class for its Lie subalgebroids, and study their properties. We also present several examples.

</details>


### [4] [Universal Hermitian Projective Calculus for CH2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26129)
*Karl J Kreder*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文为复双曲空间 $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ 在Hermitian射影模型中建立了一套代数不变量演算体系，将度量与角度量替换为射影不变量代数数据，并证明了三点Gram行列式、三角学、复测地线等核心几何量的分母消去恒等式，同时推广到带星域（包括有限Hermitian几何）上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复双曲几何中，传统度量与角度计算依赖实解析结构，缺乏统一的代数框架。本文旨在建立一个纯射影不变量代数演算，使几何量可由Hermitian配对模量、行列式四元数、极散布、三乘积相位等代数数据表示，从而简化计算并实现跨域（包括有限域）统一。

Method: 从三维Hermitian向量空间（签名(2,1)）出发，将 $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ 视为投射化负锥，边界视为投射化零锥。引入一系列代数不变量：Hermitian配对模量、行列式四元数、极散布、三乘积相位、交比不变量、接触边界形式、归一化球核、有限Hermitian入射律。通过分母消去技术证明三点Gram行列式、三角学、复测地线、平分线、脊柱球面、射影酉协变性、CR/接触图册转换及核边界极限的恒等式。

Result: 建立了完整的 $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ 射影代数不变量演算体系。三乘积相位给出了Cartan角度不变量的代数来源；配对不变量恢复了通常的Bergman距离和 $\mathbb{C}$ 上的极散布数据。所有公式可一致地组织到带星域（包括有限Hermitian几何）上，实现了复双曲几何的域统一射影演算。

Conclusion: 该工作为复双曲几何提供了一种纯代数的、域无关的射影不变量方法，不仅统一了经典复双曲几何中的计算，还通过推广到有限域打开了与有限几何、编码理论等领域的交叉可能。分母消去技术避免了传统分析中的解析困难，使几何结论在更广泛的代数域上成立。

Abstract: We develop an algebraic invariant calculus for complex hyperbolic two-space $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ in its Hermitian projective model. Starting from a three-dimensional Hermitian vector space of signature $(2,1)$, we treat $\mathbb{C}\mathrm{H}^2$ as the projectivized negative cone and its boundary as the projectivized null cone. The resulting calculus replaces metric and angular quantities by projectively invariant algebraic data: Hermitian pair moduli, determinant quadrance, polar spread, triple-product phase, cross-ratio invariants, contact boundary forms, normalized ball kernels, and finite Hermitian incidence laws. We prove denominator-cleared identities for three-point Gram determinants, triangle trigonometry, complex geodesics, bisectors, spinal spheres, projective-unitary covariance, CR/contact atlas transitions, and kernel boundary limits. The triple-product phase supplies the algebraic source of the Cartan angular invariant, while pair invariants recover the usual Bergman distance and polar-spread data over $\mathbb{C}$. The same formulas are also organized over starred fields, including finite Hermitian geometries, giving a field-uniform projective calculus for complex hyperbolic geometry.

</details>


### [5] [Arbitrarily Many Non-degenerate Local Maxima of First Nonzero Eigenfunctions on Positively Curved Two-spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26419)
*Heng Zhang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了对任意整数m≥2，存在一个微分同胚于S²、具有正高斯曲率的光滑闭黎曼曲面(M,g)，使得其第一非零Laplace特征值λ₁(M)是单重的，且归一化后的第一特征函数至少具有m个互异的非退化局部极大值，从而否定了Grossi和Provenzano提出的开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回应并否定Grossi和Provenzano (2024)提出的开放问题，该问题推测球面上具有正高斯曲率的黎曼度量可能限制第一Laplace特征函数的局部极大值数量。

Method: 通过构造具体的黎曼曲面，证明存在微分同胚于S²且具有正高斯曲率的度量，使得第一特征函数可以具有任意多个（至少m个）不同的非退化局部极大值。

Result: 成功构造了满足条件的黎曼曲面，使得第一非零Laplace特征值简单且归一化特征函数拥有至少m个不同的非退化局部极大值。

Conclusion: Grossi和Provenzano关于球面上第一Laplace特征函数局部极大值数量受限于曲率条件的开放问题被否定回答。

Abstract: We prove that, for every integer $m\ge 2$, there is a smooth closed Riemannian surface $(M,g)$ diffeomorphic to $\mathbb S^2$, with positive Gaussian curvature, such that $λ_1(M)$ is simple and, after choosing the sign, its normalized first nonzero Laplace eigenfunction has at least $m$ distinct non-degenerate local maxima. This gives a negative answer to the Open Question of Grossi and Provenzano (Math. Ann. 389(4): 3447--3470, 2024).

</details>


### [6] [Curvatures of curves in $\mathbb{R}^{2}$ endowed with a canonical linear connection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26864)
*Muhittin Evren Aydın,Rafael López*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究配备了规范线性连接的ℝ²中平面曲线的几何性质。通过引入切向曲率和测地曲率的概念，证明了给定曲率曲线的存在唯一性定理。找出所有常曲率曲线，并推广了曲率是弧长参数线性函数的曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在配备规范线性连接的ℝ²空间中，探究平面曲线的几何性质，建立该框架下曲线曲率理论的基础。

Method: 引入切向曲率和测地曲率的概念，运用微分几何方法分析曲线的存在性、唯一性及分类问题。

Result: 证明了给定曲率曲线的存在唯一性定理，找出了所有常曲率曲线，并推广了曲率为弧长参数线性函数的曲线类型。

Conclusion: 在规范线性连接的ℝ²空间中，建立了曲线曲率理论的基本框架，完善了该几何结构下曲线的分类结果。

Abstract: We investigate the geometry of plane curves in $\mathbb{R}^2$ endowed with a canonical linear connection. By introducing the notions of the tangential and geodesic curvatures, we prove the existence and uniqueness theorems for curves with prescribed curvatures. We find all curves with constant curvature and we generalize the curves whose curvatures are linear functions of the arc length parameter.

</details>


### [7] [Homogeneity actions, N-manifolds, and the Frobenius theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27135)
*Janusz Grabowski,Asier López-Gordón*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究由齐次性作用诱导分次的N-分次超流形，证明h_0是到子流形M的光滑收缩且构成纤维丛，给出齐次Frobenius定理的简洁证明，并在特定条件下与Bursztyn等人的N-流形定义等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立N-分次超流形的齐次性几何框架，统一并推广已有的N-流形理论及相关Frobenius定理。

Method: 利用乘法幺半群R的齐次性作用h_t分析流形结构，证明h_0的收缩性质和纤维丛结构，结合奇偶算子的条件进行几何刻画。

Result: 证明了h_0是到子流形M的光滑收缩且h_0: M→M是以R^{m|n}为典型纤维的纤维丛；给出了齐次Frobenius定理的简洁证明；在h_{-1}作用为奇偶算子的条件下，得到了与Bursztyn等人定义的N-流形等价的几何刻画。

Conclusion: 齐次性方法为N-分次超流形提供了统一的几何框架，其Frobenius定理推广了N-流形的相应结果。

Abstract: This paper is devoted to $\mathbb{N}$-graded supermanifolds $\mathcal{M}$ whose grading is induced by a homogeneity action, i.e., a smooth action $\mathbb{R}\ni t\mapsto h_t$ of the multiplicative monoid of real numbers on $\mathcal{M}$. We show that the map $h_0$ is a smooth retraction onto a submanifold $M=h_0(\mathcal{M})$, and that $h_0:\mathcal{M}\to M$ is a fiber bundle with typical fiber $\mathbb{R}^{m|n}$. Using this homogeneity approach, we obtain a simple proof of a homogeneous version of the Frobenius theorem. If, in addition, $h_{-1}$ acts as the parity operator on $\mathcal{M}$, we provide a geometric characterization equivalent to the recent definition of $\mathbb{N}$-manifolds due to Bursztyn, Cueca, and Mehta in terms of sheaves of graded algebras with prescribed local models. As a consequence, the homogeneous Frobenius theorem for $\mathbb{N}$-manifolds proved by these authors appears as a special case of our more general result.

</details>


### [8] [Asymptotics of the Selberg Zeta function on the spin moduli space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27152)
*Cipriana Anghel,Sergiu Moroianu,Rareş Stan*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在退化过程中，Selberg zeta函数对旋量Dirac算子的对数导数的渐近展开，证明了当某些简单闭测地线长度光滑收敛到0时，展开式可达$t^4\log t$阶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在双曲度量退化（由捏合过程导致）时，Selberg zeta函数的渐近行为，特别是对旋量Dirac算子的情形。

Method: 通过对紧致曲面上旋量Dirac算子的Selberg zeta函数的对数导数进行渐近分析，考虑一族退化双曲度量，其中某些不相交简单闭测地线的长度$l_j(t)$在$t\to0$时光滑趋于0。

Result: 证明了该对数导数存在一个有限的渐近展开，最高阶项达到$t^4\log t$。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了在度量退化（从紧致双曲曲面退化到带有尖点的完全双曲度量）过程中，Selberg zeta函数的对数导数的渐近行为，为理解该几何变化对谱理论的影响提供了精确分析。

Abstract: We prove a limited asymptotic expansion up to order $t^4\log t$ of the logarithmic derivative of the Selberg zeta function for the spin Dirac operator on compact surfaces for families of hyperbolic metrics degenerating towards complete hyperbolic metrics with cusps in a pinching process where the lengths $l_j(t)$ of certain disjoint simple closed geodesics converge smoothly to $0$ as $t\to 0$.

</details>


### [9] [Riemannian Penrose Inequality for Manifolds with Corners via Non-Linear Potential Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27155)
*Virginia Agostiniani,Christina Karapiperi,Lorenzo Mazzieri*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文针对三维渐近平直黎曼流形中跨越超曲面Σ的度量非C¹光滑情形，给出了正质量定理和Riemann-Penrose不等式的全新证明。与依赖光滑度量原始结论的Miao和McCormick-Miao方法不同，本文直接恢复这些结果，并基于Agostiniani-Mantegazza-Mazzieri-Oronzio量的近似单调性建立统一论证框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对非光滑度量(度量在超曲面Σ上非C¹)的正质量定理和Riemann-Penrose不等式证明依赖于它们光滑度量的原始结论，缺乏直接且统一的论证方法。

Method: 建立Agostiniani-Mantegazza-Mazzieri-Oronzio引入量的近似单调性，结合Miao的逼近方案，针对Σ上具有C^{2,α}正则性的度量进行统一推理。

Result: 直接恢复正质量定理和Riemann-Penrose不等式在非光滑度量情形下的结论，无需依赖光滑度量的原始证明。

Conclusion: 提供了一种统一、直接的证明框架，适用于两种几何不等式在非光滑度量设定下的成立性验证。

Abstract: We present a new proof of the Positive Mass Theorem and the Riemannian Penrose Inequality for three-dimensional asymptotically flat Riemannian manifolds whose metrics fail to be $C^1$ across a hypersurface $Σ$, first proven by Miao and McCormick-Miao, respectively. Unlike these approaches, ours recovers these results directly, without relying on their original formulations for smooth metrics. The proofs are based on a unified argument which applies to both theorems. We achieve this by establishing an approximate monotonicity for the quantity introduced by Agostiniani-Mantegazza-Mazzieri-Oronzio, employing the approximation scheme of Miao, for metrics with $C^{2,α}$ regularity up to $Σ$.

</details>


### [10] [A non-convergence phenomenon for the CR Yamabe flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27164)
*Claudio Afeltra,Andrea Pinamonti,Pak Tung Ho*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文构造了三维CR流形上的接触形式，使得CR Yamabe流无法收敛。具体而言，在标准CR三维球面的小Rossi形变上，展示了对应的CR Yamabe流发展出单气泡集中现象的实例。该构造基于Rossi球面上伪埃尔米特质量的负性，表明质量正性不仅仅是已知CR Yamabe流收敛结果中的技术性假设，而是与流的大时间动力学本质相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究CR Yamabe流是否总是收敛，特别是在质量非正的情况下，检验质量正性假设的必要性。

Method: 通过构造标准CR三维球面的小Rossi形变，利用Rossi球面上伪埃尔米特质量的负性，设计出CR Yamabe流产生单气泡集中现象的接触形式。

Result: 成功构造了CR Yamabe流不收敛的实例，该流表现出单气泡集中（one-bubble concentration）的动力学行为。

Conclusion: 伪埃尔米特质量的正性并非仅仅是技术性假设，而是决定CR Yamabe流大时间动力学的本质条件；质量负性会导致流无法收敛。

Abstract: We construct a contact form on a three dimensional CR manifold such that the CR Yamabe flow fails to converge. More precisely, on small Rossi deformations of the standard CR three-sphere, we exhibit an example whose corresponding CR Yamabe flow develops a one-bubble concentration regime.
  The construction is based on the negativity of the pseudohermitian mass on the Rossi spheres. This shows that mass positivity is not merely a technical assumption in the known convergence results for the CR Yamabe flow, but is genuinely connected to the large-time dynamics of the flow.

</details>


### [11] [A Precompactness theorem for Einstein metrics on homogeneous torus bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27329)
*Anusha M. Krishnan,Vincent P. N. Wolff,Masoumeh Zarei*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究齐性环面丛全空间上的爱因斯坦度量，通过允许迷向群的不同嵌入，构造了以单连通空间为底、固定维数环面为纤维的无穷族单连通齐性空间。利用下降到公共底空间的方法，建立了一组估计，并证明了这些族中爱因斯坦流形的预紧性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究齐性环面丛上爱因斯坦度量的存在性与紧性理论，特别是通过迷向群不同嵌入构造无穷族结构，为理解爱因斯坦流形的模空间提供理论基础。

Method: 采用齐性空间方法，分析迷向群嵌入对全空间几何的影响；通过下降到公共底空间的技术，建立关键估计量；运用预紧性分析框架证明紧性定理。

Result: 成功建立了适用于无穷族齐性环面丛的估计体系，并证明了这些族中爱因斯坦流形满足预紧性定理。

Conclusion: 该工作为齐性环面丛上的爱因斯坦度量研究提供了新的技术工具和紧性结果，对理解更广泛的齐性爱因斯坦流形分类有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate Einstein metrics on the total space of homogeneous torus bundles. Allowing for different embeddings of the isotropy group gives rise to infinite families of simply connected homogeneous spaces fibred over a common simply connected base, with toral fibres of fixed dimension. Descending to the common base, we establish a set of estimates that we use to prove a precompactness theorem for Einstein manifolds in these families.

</details>


### [12] [Classification of homogeneous almost complex $4$-manifolds with non-degenerate torsion bundle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27336)
*Cristina Bozzetti,Costantino Medori,Lorenzo Sillari*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有非退化扭丛的殆复4-流形的局部与整体几何，揭示了其刚性导致可平行化的J-适应双覆盖，并在齐性情形下给出了完整分类：微分同胚于带有非退化扭丛殆复结构的4维李群，或透镜空间L(4,1)与ℝ或𝕋的乘积。同时确定了所有允许该结构的实4维李代数，并通过显式不变结构实现了每个可容许代数，从而彻底解决了4维存在性问题。还将这些结构与Nijenhuis-Engel结构联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究具有非退化扭丛的殆复4-流形的几何刚性与分类，特别是齐性情形下的完整刻画，并解决该结构的存在性问题。

Method: 利用刚性推导J-适应双覆盖的可平行化性质，施加拓扑约束；在齐性设定下进行分类；通过李代数分类确定可容许代数；用显式不变结构实现构造；与Engel结构的联系分析。

Result: 完整分类了齐性情形：微分同胚于带有非退化扭丛殆复结构的4维李群，或L(4,1)×ℝ或L(4,1)×𝕋；确定了所有可容许的实4维李代数；通过显式构造解决了存在性问题；建立了与Nijenhuis-Engel结构的关联。

Conclusion: 在4维情形下，具有非退化扭丛的殆复流形在齐性设定中已被完全分类，存在性问题已彻底解决，且与Engel结构的联系为后续研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the local and global geometry of almost complex $4$-manifolds admitting non-degenerate torsion bundle. The rigidity of these structures forces a parallelizable $J$-adapted double cover, which imposes severe topological constraints on the underlying manifold. Exploiting this rigidity, we give a complete classification in the homogeneous setting. We show that such a manifold is diffeomorphic either to a $4$-dimensional Lie group carrying an almost complex structure with non-degenerate torsion bundle, or to a product $L(4,1)\times\mathbb R$ or $L(4,1)\times\mathbb T$, where $L(4,1)$ is a lens space. We also determine exactly which real $4$-dimensional Lie algebras admit such a structure. Constructively, we realize every admissible algebra by an explicit invariant structure, thereby closing the existence question in dimension $4$. We also relate these structures to certain Engel structures that we call Nijenhuis--Engel, and answer the resulting existence questions in the homogeneous case.

### [13] [Observable strong field effects of extra spacetime dimension in the braneworld black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26152)
*K. K. Nandi,R. N. Izmailov,R. Kh. Karimov,A. A. Potapov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究Randall-Sundrum膜世界模型中由额外维度产生的潮汐荷Υ对DMPR膜黑洞强场透镜观测和准正则模频率的影响，发现潮汐荷能显著改变Schwarzschild黑洞的透镜观测值和QNM频率，其中DMPR−黑洞具有更低的Pretorius-Khurana临界指数γ（更强的Lyapunov不稳定性），暗示其吸积盘更亮，并利用SgrA*黑洞阴影对Υ进行了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弦论膜世界图像中额外维度在强引力（短距离）实验中的可观测效应，特别是Randall-Sundrum膜世界模型中第五维在有效爱因斯坦场方程中引入的潮汐荷Υ对黑洞物理观测量的影响。

Method: 对DMPR±两种潮汐荷修正的Schwarzschild黑洞（Υ≠0）进行强场透镜观测量的理论计算，在eikonal极限下比较二者的环down准正则模（QNM）频率，并利用SgrA*黑洞的EHT阴影观测对Υ进行约束。

Result: 潮汐荷能显著改变Schwarzschild黑洞的透镜观测值和QNM频率；DMPR−黑洞的Pretorius-Khurana临界指数γ低于Schwarzschild黑洞（即更强的Lyapunov不稳定性），暗示其吸积盘更亮；通过SgrA*黑洞阴影对Υ给出了可能的约束。

Conclusion: 膜世界模型中的潮汐荷作为额外维度的印记，在强引力透镜和引力波观测中产生可区分于标准Schwarzschild黑洞的观测特征，为检验额外维度理论提供了潜在的观测窗口。

Abstract: Inspired by the string theory, the braneworld picture introduces extra dimensions beyond the four that may have observable non-trivial effects in short distance (strong field) gravity experiments. A case in point is the Randall-Sundrum braneworld picture that projects the $5d$ bulk Weyl tensor onto the $3d$ brane providing a stress tensor in the effective Einstein field equations on the brane. Dadhich, Maartens, Papadopoulos and Rezania (DMPR) derived an exact braneworld black hole solution of the brane vacuum field equations. The solution formally resembles that of Reissner-Nordström but is physically different from it since the "tidal charge" $Υ$ in the solution is not the electric charge but an imprint from the fifth dimension allowing both signs in the power law modification $\pm \frac{Υ^{2}}{r^{2}}$ to the Schwarzschild metric $\left( Υ= 0\right)$. The corresponding black holes are designated as DMPR$\pm$. We study here the effect of $Υ$ on strong field lensing observables and compare in the eikonal limit the ring down quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies of DMPR$-$ with those of DMPR$+$, the two variants of tidal charge modified Schwarzschild black hole ($Υ= 0$). It turns out that the tidal charge can significantly modify the Schwarzschild lensing observables and QNM frequencies. In particular, we find that the Pretorius-Khurana critical exponent $γ$ of circular null orbits in the DMPR$-$ black hole has a lower value than that for the Schwarzschild black hole, which indicates a stronger Lyapunov instability suggesting that the accretion disks of DMPR$-$ black holes would appear brighter. The case of the SgrA* black hole is considered for a possible constraint on $Υ$ from the EHT observation of its shadow size.

</details>


### [14] [Charged Axially Symmetric Exponential Metric: Exact Solutions to the Einstein-Maxwell Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26160)
*S. Habib Mazharimousavi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦框架下，构建并分析了轴对称指数度规（Curzon-Chazy时空）的带电和磁化扩展，通过直接求解场方程、Harrison变换、Ehlers变换等方法，系统生成了带电、磁化、旋转（含NUT荷）的精确解，并验证了各变换之间的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Weyl类中扩展已知的轴对称Curzon-Chazy时空，研究其在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论下的带电、磁化和引力磁荷（NUT荷）精确解，以揭示这些荷如何通过精确解生成技术系统性地出现。

Method: 首先直接求解耦合场方程得到精确带电轴对称指数度规（dyonic monopole）；再用Harrison变换在Ernst形式论中重新推导该带电解，验证等价性；接着应用磁Harrison变换获得Melvin型磁化变形；最后实施Ehlers变换生成含NUT荷的稳态几何，并进一步结合磁Harrison变换得到磁化旋转（NUT型）时空。

Result: 得到了带电Curzon-Chazy时空精确解，其在无荷极限下平滑退化为真空CCS，在特殊参数下退化为极端Reissner-Nordström时空；通过Harrison变换重新导出了相同带电解；获得了Melvin型磁化变形；通过Ehlers变换生成了含非零NUT荷的旋转几何，并用Komar对偶质量进行了不变性识别；最终得到了磁化旋转（NUT型）时空。

Conclusion: 电、磁和引力磁荷（NUT荷）可以通过精确解生成技术从Curzon-Chazy时空系统地产生，展示了Weyl类中轴对称指数度规在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦框架下的丰富扩展结构。

Abstract: We construct and analyze charged and magnetized extensions of the axially symmetric exponential metric, that is known as the Curzon-Chazy spacetime (CCS) within the Weyl class. Working within the Einstein-Maxwell framework, we first derive an exact charged axially symmetric exponential metric by directly solving the coupled field equations for a dyonic monopole configuration. The solution is shown to reduce smoothly to the vacuum CCS in the neutral limit and to the extremal Reissner-Nordström spacetime in a special parameter regime. We then rederive the same charged geometry using the Harrison transformation in the Ernst formalism, establishing the equivalence between the direct and solution-generating approaches. Subsequently, we apply the magnetic Harrison transformation to obtain a Melvin-type magnetized deformation of the spacetime. Finally, by implementing the Ehlers transformation, we generate a stationary but nonrotating swirling geometry endowed with a nonvanishing NUT charge, which we identify invariantly via the Komar dual mass. A further magnetic Harrison transformation yields a magnetized swirling (NUT-type) spacetime. These results demonstrate how electric, magnetic, and gravitomagnetic charges arise systematically from the CCS through exact solution-generating techniques.

*Chengjia Chen,Yin Hao,Zelin Zhang,Qiyuan Pan,Jiliang Jing*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用视界尺度成像探测强场区时空几何，检验引力理论；CFM黑洞含额外潮汐参数，为探索额外维度效应提供独特探针。

Method: 进行广义相对论辐射转移（GRRT）模拟，生成与M87* EHT观测一致的合成图像；采用归一化互相关系数和DSSIM指数进行图像比较分析。

Result: 潮汐参数对图像形态产生非单调变化；图像比较指标（归一化互相关系数与DSSIM指数）的不匹配量级达10^3。

Conclusion: 即使未来ngEHT和BHEX等观测设备升级，通过黑洞图像识别膜世界黑洞仍面临显著挑战。

Abstract: Horizon-scale imaging acts as a transformative tool for probing spacetime geometry, enabling stringent tests of gravitational theories in the strong-field regime. The Casadio-Fabbri-Mazzacurati(CFM) black hole in braneworld contains an extra parameter that characterizes the tidal effects from the bulk geometry, making it highly valuable for this task. We perform general relativistic radiative transfer (GRRT) simulations and generate synthetic images consistent with Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87*. We find that the tidal parameter imprints nonmonotonic changes on the image morphology, underscoring the intricate coupling between spacetime geometry and the observable radiation from the accreting plasma. We also analyze the image-comparison metric using normalized cross-correlation coefficients and the DSSIM index and find that the magnitudes of these mismatches are on the order of 10^3, which implies that identifying braneworld black holes through black hole images remains challenging even with future ngEHT and BHEX observations.

### [16] [Electrically Charged Distorted Black Holes: Thermodynamics, Particle Dynamics, and Quasinormal Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26174)
*Gamal G. L. Nashed,Salvatore Capozziello*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用Harrison变换构建了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中带电扭曲黑洞时空的精确解，分析了其热力学性质、带电测试粒子运动、黑洞阴影、类光准正则模以及带电标量扰动，发现扭曲参数和电荷对可观测效应有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中构造带电扭曲黑洞时空的精确解，并系统研究其热力学、粒子动力学、光学和扰动特征，以理解电荷与扭曲背景的耦合效应。

Method: 采用Harrison变换将电磁场引入静态扭曲真空几何，保持种子度规的径向结构；利用有效势方法研究粒子运动；通过几何光学计算黑洞阴影；采用WKB方法估算准正则模频谱。

Result: Killing视界由种子度规唯一确定，不被电荷移动；热力学量由几何扇区主导，电荷通过电磁势扩展相空间；扭曲参数改变圆形轨道并移动ISCO位置；扭曲使光子球外推，增大阴影尺寸；视界处电势为零阻止了带电超辐射放大；电磁相互作用通过规范不变组合(ω-q_s ξ_t)偏移振荡频率。

Conclusion: 带电扭曲黑洞的热力学由几何主导，电荷扩展相空间；扭曲参数显著影响粒子轨道、阴影和扰动模式；缺乏视界电势导致超辐射放大被抑制；光子轨道与领先eikonal准正则模之间存在几何对应关系。

Abstract: We construct an exact solution for the electrically charged extension of a distorted black hole spacetime within Einstein-Maxwell theory using the Harrison transformation. The resulting solution represents a charged deformation of a static distorted vacuum geometry in which the electromagnetic field is introduced through a nonlinear transformation preserving the radial structure of the seed spacetime. Consequently, the Killing horizon remains determined solely by the seed metric and it is not shifted by the electric charge. We analyze the thermodynamic properties of the solution and show that the horizon area, entropy, and temperature are governed by the geometric sector, while the electric charge enlarges the thermodynamic phase space through the electromagnetic potential. The motion of charged test particles is studied using the effective potential formalism, where the distortion parameter modifies circular orbits and shifts the location of the innermost stable circular orbit. We also investigate the black hole shadow for a static observer at finite distance and show that the distortion parameter displaces the photon sphere outward, increasing the apparent shadow size. A geometric correspondence between the photon orbit, determining the shadow and the leading eikonal quasinormal-mode frequency, is discussed, linking optical and perturbative observables. Finally, we study charged scalar perturbations and show that the vanishing horizon electric potential prevents a charged superradiant amplification. In the weak-coupling regime, the quasinormal-mode spectrum is estimated using the WKB method, where the electromagnetic interaction enters through the gauge-invariant combination $(ω- q_s ξ_t)$ and shifts the oscillation frequencies of the perturbations.

</details>


### [17] [Gravitational Wave Signatures from Periodic Orbits around a Non--commutative Schwarzschild Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26182)
*N. Heidari,A. A. Araújo Filho,I. P. Lobo,V. B. Bezerra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了非对易Schwarzschild黑洞周围大质量粒子的运动及周期轨道产生的引力波辐射。非对易修正使特征轨道（如ISCO）向更小半径偏移并降低角动量。通过S2星的近日点进动得到初步约束Θ/M²<0.014。引力波极化计算显示相位偏移和振幅增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非对易几何对黑洞附近粒子动力学和引力波辐射的影响，探索非对易效应的可观测特征。

Method: 分析有效势、边界轨道和ISCO；通过有理参数q对周期轨道分类；利用绝热和数值kludge近似计算引力波极化。

Result: 非对易修正使特征轨道半径和角动量减小；(E,L)平面允许区域下移；S2星近日点进动给出约束Θ/M²<0.014；引力波振幅增强并出现相位偏移。

Conclusion: 非对易效应会导致更紧密束缚的轨道构型和更紧凑的zoom-whirl结构，并通过引力波观测提供检验非对易几何的潜在途径。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate massive particle motion and the gravitational wave emission generated by periodic trajectories around a non--commutative \textit{Schwarzschild} black hole sourced by a Lorentzian matter distribution. We analyze the effective potential, the marginally bound orbit, and the innermost stable circular orbit, showing that non--commutative corrections shift these characteristic orbits toward smaller radii and reduce their corresponding angular momenta. The allowed region in the $(E, L)$ plane is also displaced toward lower values, favoring more tightly bound configurations. Periodic trajectories are classified through the rational parameter $q$, which relates the radial and azimuthal frequencies. For a fixed orbital topology, increasing the non--commutative parameter lowers the energy required to produce the orbit and results in more compact zoom--whirl configurations. Small deviations from the periodic energies are also shown to generate precessional drift. From the periastron advance of the S2 star around Sgr~A$^*$, we obtain the preliminary bound $Θ/M^{2}<0.014$. Finally, using the adiabatic and numerical kludge approximations, we compute the gravitational wave polarizations and find phase shifts and an overall enhancement of the amplitude.

</details>


### [18] [Extended Thermodynamics and Throttling Process of Charged AdS Black Holes in ModMax-dRGT Massive Gravity with Sharma-Mittal Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26210)
*Naba Jyoti Gogoi,Hassan Hassanabadi,Himasri Pinapothu,Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在ModMax非线性电动力学与dRGT-like大质量引力框架下，研究了四维带电反德西特黑洞的扩展热力学，包括焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀和P-V临界性。利用广义Sharma-Mittal熵处理非广延统计关联，推导了修正的霍金温度、比热、焦耳-汤姆逊系数和状态方程。结果表明：ModMax场的共形非线性通过将反转转变移至更小视界半径扩大了冷却域；Sharma-Mittal参数决定局部热力学稳定性，而全局反转相边界由大质量引力子背景主导；吉布斯自由能展示了类范德瓦尔斯一级相变。ModMax非线性、Sharma-Mittal参数和大质量引力在临界区域中呈现清晰的物理解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非广延统计（Sharma-Mittal熵）与非线性电动力学（ModMax）及大质量引力理论相结合，探索在扩展相空间中黑洞热力学相变行为的完整图景，揭示不同理论修正对热力学现象的区分性影响。

Method: 在扩展相空间中使用广义Sharma-Mittal熵，通过解析推导获得修正的霍金温度、比热、焦耳-汤姆逊系数及状态方程，并分析吉布斯自由能的相变结构。

Result: ModMax参数γ通过抑制电磁相互作用扩大冷却域；Sharma-Mittal参数(δ,R)控制局部稳定性和反转半径；全局反转相边界由大质量引力子主导。吉布斯自由能显示类范德瓦尔斯一级相变，且三种修正效应在临界区域中物理解耦。

Conclusion: 不同理论修正（非线性电动力学、非广延统计、大质量引力）对黑洞热力学相行为产生可区分的特征性影响，可作为诊断黑洞物理中非线性与非广延修正的鲁棒工具。

Abstract: We investigate the extended thermodynamics, including the Joule-Thomson expansion and $P-V$ criticality, of a four-dimensional charged anti-de Sitter (AdS) black hole within the combined framework of ModMax nonlinear electrodynamics and dRGT-like massive gravity. Operating in the extended phase space and employing the generalised Sharma-Mittal entropy to account for non-extensive statistical correlations, we derive exact analytical expressions for the modified Hawking temperature, specific heat, Joule-Thomson coefficient, and the equation of state. Our analysis of the throttling process reveals that the conformal nonlinearities of the ModMax field ($γ$) expand the physically accessible cooling domain by shifting the inversion transition to smaller horizon radii. While the Sharma-Mittal parameters ($δ$, $R$) critically govern local thermodynamic stability and the inversion radius, the global inversion phase boundary remains fundamentally dictated by the massive graviton background. Furthermore, an analysis of the Gibbs free energy uncovers a van der Waals-like first-order phase transition characterized by a distinct swallow-tail structure. We observe a clear physical decoupling in the critical regime: ModMax nonlinearities modify the critical phase boundary by suppressing electromagnetic interactions, Sharma-Mittal parameters dictate the relative thermal stability of competing phases, and massive gravity governs the overarching macroscopic phase landscape. These results highlight the sensitivity of thermodynamic phase phenomena as robust diagnostic tools for distinguishing nonlinear and non-extensive modifications to black hole physics.

</details>


### [19] [Time-domain framework for the Teukolsky equation with a particle source using comoving hyperboloidal coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26339)
*Aditya Vaswani,Leor Barack,Oliver Long,Rodrigo Panosso Macedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于共动、空间紧致双曲坐标的1+1维Teukolsky方程时域积分方案和实现代码，该方案以点粒子为源，有效避免了非物理增长模式问题，并通过标量场和引力波测试验证了其长期稳定性，为极端质量比散射中的完全引力自作用力计算铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Teukolsky方程数值演化方案存在非物理增长模式问题，且对粒子世界线上的跳跃条件处理复杂，亟需一种稳定且简洁的数值方案来处理极端质量比系统中的引力自作用力计算。

Method: 采用共动、空间紧致双曲坐标对Teukolsky方程进行1+1维时域积分；共动坐标简化了粒子世界线上的跳跃条件施加；通过标量场在Schwarzschild背景上的圆测地线轨道和散射轨道进行测试，并对s=-2的Teukolsky方程进行实现验证。

Result: 该方案有效避免了非物理增长模式；共动坐标极大简化了跳跃条件的处理；标量场和引力波测试均展示了长期稳定性和无增长模式行为。

Conclusion: 该方法为极端质量比散射中完整引力自作用力的计算铺平了道路。

Abstract: We present a scheme and implementation code for time-domain integration of the Teukolsky equation in 1+1 dimensions with a point-particle source, based on comoving, spatially compactified hyperboloidal coordinates. We demonstrate that the scheme evades the problem of nonphysical growing modes that plague some numerical evolution schemes without compactification. Our use of comoving coordinates greatly simplifies the application of jump conditions on the particle's worldline. We develop our method and test its performance for a scalar field on a Schwarzschild background, first for a circular geodesic orbit source and then for a scattering geodesic orbit. We then present a test implementation of the method for the $s = -2$ Teukolsky equation, illustrating its long-term stability and absence of growing-mode behavior through comparison with similar results using noncompactified characteristic coordinates. Our method paves the way to calculations of the full gravitational self-force in extreme-mass-ratio scattering.

</details>


### [20] [Thermodynamics of thin-shell wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26370)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了动态薄壳虫洞的统一热力学描述，从透明真空体推广到含物质渡越喉部的情形。研究表明：孤立壳在透明演化下熵守恒（TdS=0）；有物质时广义热力学第一定律为TṠ=AΦ，熵随物质流入/流出而增减；给出了零尘埃和无质量标量场的能流表达式，讨论了霍金辐射；建立了广义第二定律；应用于零尘埃吸积时发现临界吸积率敏感依赖于时空几何和状态方程；能流涨落导致喉部随机力，形成Langevin描述和涨落-耗散关系，引起喉径扩散和额外熵产生。该框架适用于广义相对论中一大类球对称薄壳构造，为薄壳虫洞提供了一致的 thermodynamics 描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为动态薄壳虫洞建立统一的热力学描述框架，从透明真空体情形推广到包含物质穿越喉部的更一般情况，并探讨其在天体物理和引力波观测中的意义。

Method: 采用薄壳形式主义，结合热力学第一定律、熵变分析、能流计算（零尘埃、无质量标量场）、量子对产生（霍金辐射）分析，以及Langevin方程和涨落-耗散定理描述随机动力学。

Result: 透明演化下熵守恒（TdS=0）；物质存在时TṠ=AΦ，熵变方向取决于物质流向；给出了零尘埃和无质量标量场的能流表达式；发现临界吸积率强烈依赖于时空几何和壳状态方程；能流涨落诱导喉径扩散和额外熵产生。

Conclusion: 薄壳虫洞具有一致的热力学描述，其动力学对吸积过程敏感，为未来引力波探测奇特致密天体提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a unified thermodynamic description of dynamic thin-shell wormholes, starting from the transparent (vacuum bulk) case and then relaxing the transparency condition to include bulk matter crossing the throat. For isolated shells, we show that the entropy is conserved under transparent evolution, $TdS=0$, which holds for arbitrary dynamical motion of the throat within the assumptions of the thin-shell formalism. When bulk matter is present, the generalised first law becomes $T\dot{S}=AΦ$, where $Φ$ is the net energy flux; entropy increases (decreases) when matter flows into (out of) the shell. Explicit expressions for the flux are provided for null dust and massless scalar fields, and quantum pair production (Hawking-like emission) is also discussed. A formulation of the generalised second law is presented, and it is consistent with standard thermodynamic expectations under conditions where heat flows from hotter to colder regions. As a concrete astrophysical application, we study accretion of null dust: the critical accretion rate above which the throat becomes dynamically unstable depends sensitively on the spacetime geometry and the shell equation of state, highlighting the environmental dependence of these configurations. Fluctuations in the energy flux induce a stochastic force on the throat dynamics, leading to a Langevin description with an associated fluctuation-dissipation relation. This results in diffusion of the throat radius and additional entropy production. The framework applies to a broad class of spherically symmetric thin-shell constructions within general relativity. Our results provide evidence that thin-shell wormholes admit a consistent thermodynamic description, quantify their sensitivity to accretion processes, and suggest possible avenues for probing exotic compact objects with future gravitational wave observations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究正则黑洞（尤其是Hayward黑洞）时空中狄拉克场的量子关联特性，以及奇点正则化与量子信息保护之间的潜在联系。

Method: 采用Wootters concurrence和CHSH贝尔参数，分析惯性观测者与近地平线观测者之间共享纠缠态在霍金辐射影响下的变化，对比费米子与玻色子的差异。

Abstract: We investigate bipartite quantum correlations of Dirac fields in the spacetime of a Hayward regular black hole. Using the Wootters concurrence and the CHSH Bell parameter, we analyze the influence of Hawking radiation on an entangled state shared by an inertial observer and a near-horizon observer. We show that, unlike the bosonic case, fermionic correlations remain nonzero even in the infinite-temperature limit owing to the Pauli exclusion principle, while part of the entanglement is redistributed to inaccessible modes inside the horizon. The accessible modes exhibit Bell nonlocality for all finite Hawking temperatures, whereas the interior modes never violate Bell's inequality. The Hayward regularity parameter $g$ affects the correlations only through the Hawking temperature, whose decrease with increasing $g$ enhances the preservation of quantum information. These results suggest a close connection between singularity resolution and the robustness of fermionic quantum correlations in regular black-hole spacetimes.

### [22] [Stueckelberg Gauge Invariant Formulation of MOG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26427)
*John W. Moffat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了修正引力理论（MOG）的Stueckelberg规范不变形式。通过引入补偿标量场使有质量矢量场具有规范不变性，无需希格斯场、自发对称破缺或真空期望值来固定有效牛顿引力耦合。这分离了矢量质量的规范不变起源与引力耦合的宇宙学演化，保持了MOG的有限程矢量相互作用，同时允许有效引力耦合作为独立标量或尺度依赖量处理。该公式为MOG与核合成、宇宙微波背景、大尺度结构、引力透镜和距离数据的比较提供了规范不变框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统MOG理论中矢量场的质量生成依赖于对称性破缺机制，这导致有效牛顿引力耦合与宇宙学演化紧密绑定。为了在宇宙学检验中解耦这两个因素，需要一个规范不变的框架，使矢量质量源于Stueckelberg机制而非希格斯机制，从而独立处理引力耦合的演化和早期宇宙约束。

Method: 采用Stueckelberg机制引入补偿标量场，构造有质量矢量场的规范不变拉格朗日量，无需自发对称破缺或真空期望值。通过该形式化方法分离矢量质量的规范不变起源与有效引力耦合的宇宙学演化。

Result: 建立了MOG的Stueckelberg规范不变形式，保持了有限程矢量相互作用的核心特征，同时使有效引力耦合可作为独立量处理。该框架适用于宇宙学检验，能兼容早期宇宙（核合成、CMB）与晚期大尺度结构（引力透镜、距离数据）的约束。

Abstract: We develop a Stueckelberg gauge-invariant formulation of modified gravity (MOG). The massive vector field is made gauge-invariant by introducing a compensating scalar field, without requiring a Higgs field, spontaneous symmetry breaking, or a vacuum expectation value to fix the effective Newtonian gravitational coupling. This separates the gauge-invariant origin of the vector mass from the cosmological evolution of the gravitational coupling. The formulation preserves the finite-range vector interaction of MOG, while allowing the effective gravitational coupling to be treated as an independent scalar or scale-dependent quantity. This distinction is important for cosmological tests, since early-universe constraints and late-time large-scale gravitational phenomena need not be tied to a symmetry-breaking vacuum. The Stueckelberg formulation provides a gauge-invariant framework for comparing MOG with nucleosynthesis, cosmic microwave background, large-scale structure, lensing, and distance data.

### [24] [A Shortest-Path Anisotropy Diagnostic for Black-Hole Graph Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27248)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何从图的路径结构（最短路径多重性）中提取弯曲空间的几何信息，特别是发展一种适用于黑洞几何图离散化的曲率敏感诊断工具。

Method: 定义基于最短路径数目立方平均偏差的壳基各向异性统计量，在多种黑洞嵌入几何的图离散化上进行测试，并与平面对照几何进行比较，通过随机种子平均和参数扫描验证稳健性。

Result: 该统计量在黑洞几何中呈现与对数Kretschmann标量强关联的稳定径向分布；平面对照不重现该趋势；在Reissner-Nordström、Bardeen和Hayward参数扫描中展现出稳健性；但在非黑洞基准曲面上并非通用的逐点曲率标量。

Abstract: Graph-based representations of curved spaces offer a way to probe how geometric information is encoded in shortest-path structure. In this work, we introduce a shell-based shortest-path anisotropy statistic for graph discretizations of embedded spatial slices of black-hole geometries. The statistic is based on the cubic mean deviation of the logarithm of the number of shortest paths from a reference vertex to vertices on a graph-distance shell. We test the diagnostic on graph discretizations of static, spherically symmetric black-hole embedding geometries, including Schwarzschild/Flamm, Reissner--Nordström, Bardeen, and Hayward backgrounds. Across these black-hole families, the statistic exhibits a stable radial organization that is strongly associated with the logarithmic Kretschmann profile, while matched-flat controls do not reproduce the same trend. For Reissner-Nordström geometries with $M=1/2$ and charges $Q=0,\ldots,0.4$, the seed-averaged radial and curvature-profile correlations remain stable over ten random seeds. Similar robustness is found for Bardeen and Hayward parameter scans. Additional tests on non-black-hole benchmark surfaces indicate that the statistic is not a universal pointwise curvature scalar; rather, it is a curvature-sensitive graph diagnostic whose interpretation depends on the graph construction and control geometry. These results suggest that shortest-path multiplicity anisotropy can provide a useful probe of curvature-organized structure in graph discretizations of black-hole embedding geometries.

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了早期宇宙中具有体粘滞性的背景下原初黑洞的形成，发现体粘滞性会系统性提高坍缩阈值（约与粘滞强度ε线性相关）并增强近阈值坍缩产生的黑洞质量，从而改变原初黑洞的形成阈值与质量标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，在具有体粘滞性的宇宙学背景下研究原初黑洞形成。通过设定不同体粘滞强度ε和状态方程参数w，测定坍缩临界阈值μ_c，并拟合近阈值坍缩的标准临界标度律来分析黑洞质量。

Result: 1) 临界阈值μ_c对状态方程参数w的依赖关系与无粘滞情况类似；2) μ_c随体粘滞强度ε增加而近似线性增大；3) 体粘滞性导致近阈值坍缩产生的原初黑洞质量增强。

Conclusion: 体粘滞性可以系统性改变早期宇宙中原初黑洞的形成阈值和质量标度律，在考虑原初黑洞形成时有必要纳入体粘滞效应。

Abstract: We investigate primordial black hole (PBH) formation in a cosmological background with bulk viscosity. Using numerical simulations, we determine the collapse threshold and the resulting PBH mass. We find that the critical threshold $μ_c$ retains a dependence on the equation-of-state parameter $w$ similar to that in the inviscid case, but is enhanced by an amount comparable to the bulk-viscosity strength $ε$. For fixed $w$, the increase in $μ_c$ is approximately linear in $ε$. By fitting the standard critical-scaling law for near-threshold collapse, we find that the bulk viscosity leads to an enhancement in the resulting PBH mass. These results indicate that bulk viscosity can systematically modify both the PBH threshold and PBH mass scaling law in the early universe.

### [26] [Time-domain evolution of Lorenz-gauge metric perturbations: taming the $\ell=m=1$ gauge instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27016)
*Jonathan Thornburg*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在Schwarzschild背景时空中计算由小质量粒子扰动的Lorenz规范度规微扰的时间演化方法，通过构建与不稳定规范模式正交的微扰，成功抑制了m=1模式中线性增长的不稳定规范模式，使微扰在长时间演化中保持有界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算极端质量比旋近系统在Schwarzschild或Kerr背景黑洞中由小质量粒子源发的度规微扰是引力波研究的关键步骤，但Lorenz规范下的时间域演化中存在m=1不稳定规范模式（线性增长），需要有效方法加以抑制。

Method: 将度规微扰分解为e^{imφ}模式，提出"正交化"方法：将源发微扰与同时演化的齐次微扰进行线性组合，并"偶尔"更新组合系数，使所得微扰相对于选定的内积与齐次解正交，从而抑制不稳定规范模式成分。

Result: 在Schwarzschild圆轨道测试案例中，所得正交化微扰满足O(μ) Einstein方程和Lorenz规范条件；随时间趋于无穷时保持有界；在有限晚期时间仅含少量不稳定规范模式成分；该方法对粒子建模为微扰跳跃条件和有效源两种情况均有效。

Conclusion: 所提出的正交化方法能有效消除Lorenz规范时间域演化中的不稳定规范模式，为后续引力波计算提供了稳定的数值工具，相关代码已随文发布并存入Black Hole Perturbation Toolkit。

Abstract: Calculating the spacetime metric perturbation (MP) sourced by a small "particle" of mass $μM$ (with $0 < μ\ll 1$) moving in a Schwarzschild or Kerr "background" black hole spacetime of mass $M$ is a longstanding research area in general relativity. This calculation also has an important astrophysical motivation as a major step in calculating the gravitational waves emitted by an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral system. Here I consider the specific problem of the time-domain calculation of the $\mathcal{O}(μ)$ Lorenz-gauge MP $h_{ab}$ sourced by the particle. Decomposing the Schwarzschild-background MP into $e^{imφ}$ modes, Dolan and Barack [Phys. Rev. D 87, 084066 (2013), arXiv:1211.4586] found that the $m=1$ time-domain Lorenz-gauge MP generically contains an \emph{unstable gauge mode} which grows linearly with time. Here I demonstrate a method for computing a Lorenz-gauge time-domain evolution which is mostly free of this gauge mode. This method computes an "orthogonalized" MP $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ as a linear combination of the sourced MP and a homogeneous MP $h_{ab}^\text{hom}$ (evolved in parallel with the sourced MP). The linear combination is updated "occasionally" to make $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ orthogonal to $h_{ab}^\text{hom}$ with respect to a chosen inner product on MPs. I show that, for a Schwarzschild-circular-orbit test case, the resulting $h_{ab}^\text{ortho}$ satisfies the $\mathcal{O}(μ)$ Einstein equations and Lorenz gauge conditions, remains bounded as $t \to \infty$, and at late (finite) times contains only a small component of the unstable gauge mode. These results hold both with the particle modelled via MP jump conditions and with particle modelled by a "effective source". My numerical code for obtaining all of these results is included with this paper, and will be deposited in the Black Hole Perturbation Toolkit.

</details>

Motivation: 探究有限空腔中RN黑洞的热力学拓扑分类，并分析电荷、空腔边界和时空维度对拓扑类的影响。

Method: 从约化欧几里得作用量出发，利用准局域能量、熵和壳上逆温构建离壳矢量场，在四维和五维具体例子中进行分析。

Result: 有限空腔中，中性黑洞属于$W^{0-}$类，带电黑洞属于$W^{1+}$类；固定物理电荷下将空腔半径发送至无穷时，分类交换为中性$W^{1-}$和带电$W^{0+}$。

Conclusion: 电荷和空腔边界（而非时空维度）决定RN空腔黑洞家族的精细拓扑分类。

Abstract: We study thermodynamic topological classes of $d$-dimensional Reissner--Nordström (RN) black holes in a cavity at fixed charge. Starting from the reduced Euclidean action, we use the quasilocal energy, entropy, and on-shell inverse temperature to construct the off-shell vector field. A finite cavity gives two charge dependent classes: neutral black holes belong to $W^{0-}$, whereas charged black holes belong to $W^{1+}$. If the cavity radius is sent to infinity at fixed physical charge, the endpoint data change, giving $W^{1-}$ for the neutral case and $W^{0+}$ for the charged case. Thus the electric charge and the outer boundary, rather than the spacetime dimension in the explicit four- and five-dimensional examples, determine the refined topological class within this RN cavity family.

</details>


### [29] [Beyond the equation of state: a second-order diagnostic for dynamical dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27356)
*Bob Osano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了暗能量密度演化的二阶曲率诊断量 $\mathcal{C}=\rho_{\rm DE}''/\rho_{\rm DE}$，该量能直接探测暗能量状态方程参数的时间演化 $\omega_{\rm DE}'$，且不受相互作用强度主导。基于DESI约束的CPL模型验证表明，在$H$测量精度优于1.5%时信噪比超过3，同时自然推广了Caldwell-Linder冻结/解冻分类至相互作用暗能量模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一阶连续性方程仅依赖暗能量状态方程参数的瞬时值$\omega_{\rm DE}$，无法显式体现$\omega_{\rm DE}$的演化信息（即$\omega_{\rm DE}'$）。为直接探测暗能量动力学（即状态方程是否随时间变化），需要发展二阶描述。

Method: 对含线性耦合$Q_{AB}=\alpha\rho_A H$的双流体相互作用暗扇区模型，对连续性方程关于e-fold时间求二阶导，定义曲率诊断量$\mathcal{C}=\rho_{\rm DE}''/\rho_{\rm DE}$。在宇宙学常数极限下主导项为$\alpha^2$，偏离$\omega_{\rm DE}=-1$时产生含$-3\omega_{\rm DE}'$的修正项。在DESI约束的CPL模型上进行数值验证，并分析噪声传播。

Result: 曲率诊断量可恢复CPL模型全红移范围的$\omega_{\rm DE}'$（弱/强相互作用均适用）；当$\sigma_H/H\lesssim1.5\%$时信噪比超过3；对于$\alpha\lesssim0.1$，$\alpha$与$\omega_{\rm DE}'$之间的简并可忽略；非相互作用极限下自然恢复Caldwell-Linder冻结/解冻分类。

Conclusion: 二阶曲率诊断量为探测暗能量动力学提供了互补工具，可直接识别动力学暗能量（区别于宇宙学常数），并推广了现有分类框架至相互作用暗能量模型。

Abstract: The first-order continuity equations determine the evolution of the energy densities but depend only on the instantaneous value of the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter. Differentiating these equations with respect to e-fold time introduces the term $ω'_{\rm DE}$ explicitly, providing a second-order probe of dark-energy dynamics. Consequently, while information about the evolution of the equation of state is encoded in the full dynamical solution, it is not explicit in the first-order continuity equations evaluated at a given epoch. The second-order formulation, therefore, provides a complementary description in which the local evolution of the equation of state appears directly through the curvature of the density trajectory.
  For a two-fluid interacting dark-sector model with linear coupling $Q_{AB}=αρ_AH$, the resulting second-order equation defines a curvature diagnostic, $\mathcal{C}=ρ_{DE}''/ρ_{DE}$, whose leading contribution, in the cosmological-constant limit, is $α^2$, while departures from $ω_{DE}=-1$ generate corrections through both $δω=1+ω_{DE}$ and the distinctive term $-3ω_{DE}'$. Unlike first-order analyses, this contribution is independent of the interaction strength and directly identifies dynamical dark energy. Applying the diagnostic to a CPL model with parameters consistent with DESI constraints, we recover $ω_{DE}'$ across the full redshift range for both weak and strong interactions. Noise propagation shows that the diagnostic is detectable with signal-to-noise ratio exceeding three for $σ_H/H\lesssim1.5\%$, while the degeneracy between $α$ and $ω_{DE}'$ remains negligible for $α\lesssim0.1$. In the non-interacting limit, the formalism naturally recovers the Caldwell--Linder thawing/freezing classification and extends it to interacting dark-energy models.

### [30] [Bipartite entanglement of the primordial Majorana during inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26869)
*Ai-chen Li,Han-Qing Shi,Keyun Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究暴胀期间原始马约拉纳费米场的量子关联，发现足够轻的马约拉纳模在超视界尺度上能保持增强的双向量子性，对数负性明确展示了残余不可分离性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索费米子作为暴胀时期量子关联的探针，理解泡利统计如何影响超视界量子性的保持。

Method: 在无挠FLRW时空和轴子暴胀背景下推导双分量马约拉纳模方程，构建成对动量基下的二次哈密顿量，通过哈密顿对角化和费米子压缩形式得到相同的Bogoliubov变换，计算约化模的von Neumann熵和对数负性。

Result: 足够轻的马约拉纳模在超视界尺度上保持增强的双向量子性，对数负性明确显示残余不可分离性；泡利统计限制了每个螺旋度扇区仅为真空和单对态，希尔伯特空间有限。

Conclusion: 视界退出本身不足以抹除双模态中的量子特征，需进一步开展开放系统研究（如再加热和暴胀子诱导相互作用）来理解经典化过程。

Abstract: We use a primordial Majorana field as a fermionic probe of quantum correlations during inflation. Working in a torsion-free FLRW spacetime, we derive the two-component Majorana mode equations in an axion-inflation background and construct the corresponding quadratic Hamiltonian in the paired momentum basis. Hamiltonian diagonalization and the fermionic squeezing formalism are shown to give the same Bogoliubov transformation, providing a direct map from the Majorana mode functions to the instantaneous occupation number and to the two-mode state of each $(\boldsymbol{k},-\boldsymbol{k})$ pair. Because Fermi statistics restricts each helicity sector to the vacuum and one-pair states, the resulting Hilbert space is finite and the bipartite quantum-information measures can be evaluated explicitly. We compute the von Neumann entropy of the reduced mode and the logarithmic negativity of the Majorana pair. Both diagnostics indicate that sufficiently light Majorana modes can retain enhanced super-horizon bipartite quantumness, with the logarithmic negativity making the residual inseparability especially explicit. Our result does not by itself constitute an observational Bell test or a complete decoherence analysis; rather, it identifies a Pauli-bounded matter sector in which horizon exit alone is not sufficient to erase the quantum signature encoded in the two-mode state, thereby motivating an open-system study of how reheating and inflaton-induced interactions classicalize primordial fermionic probes.

### [31] [Magnetic monopole plasma oscillations and implications for TeV blazars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26229)
*Mariia Khelashvili,Takeshi Kobayashi,Andrew J. Long*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究磁单极子在星系际磁场中诱导的振荡效应，发现该效应会准直带电粒子轨迹，减小TeV耀变体电磁级联的偏转角与次级GeV晕的角大小。基于H.E.S.S.和Fermi-LAT观测数据，对低质量磁单极子（m≲10⁶ GeV）的通量给出了F≲6×10⁻²³ cm⁻² s⁻¹ str⁻¹的强约束，优于现有实验和天体物理上限。同时指出，若存在非零磁单极子丰度，TeV观测给出的IGMF下界需修正，磁单极子数密度越高则下界越强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索磁单极子在星系际磁场中诱导的类等离子体振荡效应，并利用该效应对磁单极子丰度施加观测约束。

Method: 理论上分析磁单极子诱导IGMF振荡对带电粒子轨迹的准直效应，进而影响TeV耀变体电磁级联的偏转角与次级GeV晕角大小；结合H.E.S.S.和Fermi-LAT对1ES 0229+200的次级晕角大小观测约束，推导磁单极子通量的上限。

Result: 对低质量磁单极子（m≲10⁶ GeV）给出通量上限F≲6×10⁻²³ cm⁻² s⁻¹ str⁻¹；若当前IGMF强度B≳10⁻¹² G，该约束弱于现有极限；非零磁单极子丰度下，IGMF下界需加强。

Conclusion: 磁单极子诱导的IGMF振荡可显著影响耀变体次级晕观测，并转化为对磁单极子丰度的新约束，同时修正IGMF的下界估计。

Abstract: Magnetic monopoles arise in many beyond Standard Model scenarios, symmetrize Maxwell's equations, and their existence would be tied to the quantization of electric charge. It has been argued that, when placed in an astrophysical magnetic field, monopoles can induce a magnetic version of plasma oscillations. In this work, we explore monopole-induced oscillations of the intergalactic magnetic field (IGMF). We show that monopole-induced oscillations of the magnetic field lead to collimation of electrically charged particle trajectories, reducing the usual deflection by the magnetic field. The collimation effect impacts the deflection angle in the electromagnetic cascades of TeV blazars and leads to a decrease in the angular size of blazar secondary GeV halos. Therefore, the constraints on the secondary halo angular size from combined H.E.S.S. and Fermi-LAT observations translate into bounds on the magnetic monopole abundance. The bounds on the magnetic monopole flux obtained in this work from blazar 1ES 0229+200, depending on the IGMF strength, can be as strong as $F \lesssim 6 \times 10^{-23}\, \text{cm}^{-2} \text{s}^{-1} \text{str}^{-1}$ for low-mass monopoles $m \lesssim 10^6\, \text{GeV}$, stronger than existing laboratory and astrophysical bounds. The bound becomes subdominant to current constraints if the present-day IGMF value is stronger than $B \gtrsim 10^{-12}\, \text{G}$. At the same time, in the case of non-zero monopole abundance, the IGMF lower bound from TeV observations itself should be revised, resulting in a stronger lower bound at higher monopole number density.

Abstract: Meson screening masses trace the dissolution of hadronic correlations in hot QCD.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于标量辐射子和纯劈裂函数的逆项构造方法；利用部分分式技术解缠多极辐射中的重叠奇异性；运动学映射采用迭代的次领头阶(NLO)运动学；数值积分中使用基于扇区分解的解析与数值混合技术处理反向配置下的相空间积分。

Conclusion: 所提出的局部红外相减方法能够有效处理NNLO QCD计算中的红外发散问题，为色单态衰变过程提供了一种可行的计算方案，数值结果验证了该方法的收敛性和正确性。

Abstract: We introduce a local infrared subtraction method for next-to-next-to-leading order QCD calculations in color singlet decays, with counterterms based on scalar radiators and pure splitting functions. Overlapping singularities in the multipole radiation pattern are disentangled by partial fractioning, and the kinematics mapping corresponds to iterated next-to-leading order kinematics. We verify that the double-real remainder to $e^+e^-\to\;q\bar{q}$ is rendered finite in the single and double unresolved limits and investigate the numerical convergence of the Monte-Carlo integral. We compute the phase-space integrals of the scalar counterterms in the back-to-back configuration, both analytically and with the help of numerical techniques based on sector decomposition.

Several reward designs are developed to guide the agent toward parameter regions producing large gravitational wave amplitudes, broad frequency coverage, and detector sensitive benchmark points. We compare the PPO scans with conventional Monte Carlo scans in both narrow and broad windows of the $U(1)_x$ vacuum expectation value. ### [37] [Kinetic freeze-out and diffusion dynamics in small-system asymmetric collisions at sqrt(sNN)=200 GeV in light of a generalized Fokker-Planck distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26301)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小系统非对称碰撞（如p-Al, p-Au, d-Au, ^3He-Au）中是否产生夸克胶子等离子体（QGP）尚存争议，传统热力学模型难以全面描述从低到高横动量区域的粒子产生。本文旨在利用广义Fokker-Planck解统一描述小系统碰撞中宽横动量范围的粒子谱，提取输运参数，探究系统尺寸和中心度对QGP性质的影响。

Method: 采用广义Fokker-Planck解（非广延统计框架）对PHENIX实验数据中的中性π介子横动量谱进行全局拟合，提取三个关键参数：有效温度T、热-硬过程转变能标、高动量区域幂律衰减指数。通过对比不同碰撞系统（p-Al, p-Au, d-Au, ^3He-Au）和不同中心度（从对心到边缘）下的参数变化，分析其与参与者数<N_part>及带电粒子赝快度密度<dN_ch/dη>的关联。

Result: 有效温度T从外围p-Al碰撞的约0.33 GeV系统性地增加到中心^3He-Au碰撞的0.45 GeV，与系统尺寸和中心度正相关。转变能标和幂律指数在不同系统和中心度下呈现一致的模式。在金靶主导碰撞几何的最大系统（^3He-Au）中，转变能标几乎不依赖于中心度，表明扩散过程达到饱和。

Conclusion: 广义Fokker-Planck解能够一致描述小系统非对称碰撞中π介子横动量谱，并灵敏探测QGP的输运性质（动量空间扩散与阻力的相对强度）和非广延动力学。即使在小系统中也存在随系统尺寸和中心度增加的更强相互作用介质，验证了小系统QGP形成的可能性。

Abstract: A generalized Fokker-Planck solution is used to examine the transverse momentum ($p_{T}$) spectra of neutral pions generated in small-system asymmetric collisions, $p$-Al, $p$-Au, $d$-Au, and $^3$He-Au, at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=200$ GeV. This framework provides a cohesive explanation of particle production over a broad range of transverse momenta. We extract the energy scale governing the transition between a thermal and a hard regime, the effective temperature ($T$), and the exponents determining the high-momentum falloff from fits to PHENIX data. $T$ increases systematically with the collision centrality and colliding system size, ranging from about 0.33 GeV in peripheral $p$-Al collisions to 0.45 GeV in central $^3$He-Au collisions. This increase is correlated with the average number of participant nucleons, $<N_{part}>$, and the charged-particle pseudorapidity density, $<dN_{ch}/dη>$, indicating that larger and more central collisions create a denser, more strongly interacting medium that freezes out at a higher temperature. The acquired transition scale and power-law exponents follow consistent patterns across systems and centralities, revealing details about the sharpness of the transition from thermal to hard processes, and the relative strength of momentum-space diffusion versus drag. Interestingly, when the gold target dominates the collision geometry in the largest system ($^3$He-Au), the transition scale becomes nearly independent of centrality, signifying saturation of the diffusion process. Our findings demonstrate that the generalized Fokker-Planck solution is a sensitive probe of transport properties and non-extensive dynamics in the quark-gluon plasma produced even in small-system relativistic collisions, and it consistently describes pion spectra in this set of collisions.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在仅含标准模型一个希格斯二重态的可重整化理论中，利用暗扇区同时实现夸克味对齐和质量层次结构的方案。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 处理无质量或不稳定粒子在中间粒子在壳时出现的发散问题，KLN定理理论上能通过求和所有物理简并过程来消除发散，但实际实施面临非连通图、广义函数、阈值行为和正则化依赖等技术挑战。

Result: 展示了多种正则化方案下复杂的抵消过程，将结果与底层的复解析结构联系起来，并朝构建有限、固定阶、包含t-道的对撞可观测量迈出了步骤。

Conclusion: KLN定理在实际应用中既有实用性，也存在许多技术微妙之处和待解决的开放问题。

Abstract: Many phenomenological calculations involving massless or unstable particles suffer from divergences as mediating particles go on-shell. One way to deal with these divergences is via the Kinoshita-Lee-Nauenberg (KLN) theorem, which guarantees that by summing over all physically-degenerate processes, the divergences cancel and inclusive observables remain finite. However, actually implementing this theorem in practice requires handling disconnected diagrams, ill-defined distributional objects, threshold behavior and subtle regulator dependence. In this work, we formulate practical prescriptions for dealing with some of these issues by studying the KLN cancellation in an illustrative model exhibiting a t-channel divergence. We demonstrate intricate cancellations across several regularization schemes, connect our results to the complex-analytic structure of the underlying amplitudes, and take steps towards constructing a finite, fixed-order, inclusive t-channel collider observable. This work highlights both the utility of the KLN theorem, and also the technical subtleties and open questions involved with applying it in practice.

### [41] [Unified study of hyperon semileptonic decays in a relativistic three-quark model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26596)
*Ru-Hui Ni,Zhen-Yang Wang,Jia-Jun Wu,Bing-Song Zou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对八重态重子半轻子衰变的理论研究不够统一，缺乏无自由参数的系统性框架来预测所有衰变通道的弱跃迁振幅和形状因子，特别是在实验数据有限的通道。

Method: 采用相对论三夸克模型（R3QM），所有重子波函数通过半相对论势模型拟合重子质量谱确定，从而使得弱跃迁振幅的计算没有自由参数。利用相同波函数计算分支比和轻子普适性比率，并计算完整八重态跃迁形状因子。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个将八重态重子弱形状因子与夸克层次重子的自旋-味和空间结构联系起来的框架，并为未来重子半轻子衰变测量提供了可检验的弱流可观测量。

Abstract: We present a unified theoretical study of semileptonic decays of ground-state octet hyperons using the relativistic three-quark model (R3QM). A key innovation of our approach is that all baryon wave functions are determined by fitting the baryon mass spectrum with a semirelativistic potential model, leading to predictions for weak transition amplitudes without free parameters. With the same wave functions, we calculate the branching fractions and lepton flavor universality ratios for the octet channels. The calculated values agree with the available experimental data and give predictions for channels with limited experimental information. We further compute the complete set of octet transition form factors without any additional free parameters, so that the weak current can be examined beyond the rate observables. In the well-measured $Λ\to p \ell^-\barν_\ell$ channel, the calculated leading vector and axial-vector form factors, $f_1(0)$ and $g_1(0)$, agree well with recent lattice QCD results, and the $g_1/f_1$ ratio is consistent with recent BESIII measurements. Beyond the leading vector and axial-vector terms, the complete form factor set separates the weak magnetism, second class, and the pole contribution associated with the partially conserved axial current (PCAC) relation. The weak magnetism term $f_2$ shows the clearest channel dependence compared with lattice QCD results, and its smaller values in some channels may point to transverse current strength not fully saturated by pure $qqq$ valence components. This work provides a framework for connecting octet hyperon weak form factors to the spin--flavor and spatial structure of baryons at the quark level, and gives testable weak current observables for future hyperon semileptonic decay measurements.

We employ two complementary probes, the falling-string and shooting-string descriptions, to compute the stopping distance and the instantaneous energy loss of a light quark moving either transverse or parallel to the rotation axis. We find that increasing the temperature or the parameter $a$ reduces the stopping distance and enhances the instantaneous energy loss. The effect of $a$ is more pronounced for transverse motion than for motion along the rotation axis, indicating an anisotropic energy-loss pattern induced by the spinning/boosted background. Method: 采用Abelian-Higgs模型与Majorana费米子耦合的宇宙弦模型，费米子质量由Higgs场产生，模型基于规范化的U(1)_{B-L}理论框架。将Majorana费米子识别为右手中微子，并纳入粒子辐射导致的能量损失机制，计算并分析SGWB光谱。

Result: 评估了考虑粒子辐射能量损失后的SGWB光谱，发现了由于粒子辐射导致的非常高频率截断现象。

Conclusion: 宇宙弦的粒子辐射会对SGWB光谱产生显著影响，特别是在高频区域出现截断，这为通过引力波观测研究宇宙弦和粒子物理模型提供了新的可观测特征。

Abstract: The effect of particle radiation on the spectrum of the stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) from cosmic strings is studied. We consider cosmic strings in an Abelian-Higgs model coupling with Majorana fermion whose mass is generated by the Higgs field, motivated by a gauged $U(1)_{B-L}$ model, in which the Majorana fermions are identified with right-handed neutrinos. Taking the energy loss by particle radiation into account, we evaluate the resultant SGWB spectrum and demonstrate the emergence of very high frequency cutoff due to the particle radiation.

### [46] [Thermodynamical analysis of QGP using effective PNJL model with Quasiparticle approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26956)
*Yogesh Kumar,Himanshu Aggarwal,R. S. Laishram,Poonam Jain,Om Prakash,Sanjay Tyagi,Pargin Bangotra,Vinod Kumar,Yagyadatta Goswami,M. K. Sahu*

Conclusion: 准粒子模型扩展将PNJL从描述性工具提升为更具定性意义的唯象方法，改善了对强相互作用QGP的描述；两种变体的相互一致性验证了准粒子机制的物理基础，增强了所计算状态方程的可信度。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics of the quark-gluon plasma using an effective Two flavor Polyakov Nambu Jona Lasinio (PNJL) model extended by a quasiparticle description for quarks and gluons, incorporating temperature dependent quark masses within the PNJL framework. Two variants, Quasiparticle Model-I and Quasiparticle Model-II, are implemented to investigate bulk thermodynamic observables such as pressure, energy density, entropy density, specific heat, and the speed of sound. The combined framework yields a robust baseline for the description of hot QGP dynamics in the high temperature regime at vanishing chemical potential and zero magnetic field. Systematic comparison with lattice QCD results shows an excellent agreement and clear improvement over conventional PNJL implementations. We observe that both variants complement each other, offering mutually consistent insight into quasiparticle mass effects and medium response in the deconfined phase. This mutual consistency validates the physical foundation of the overall quasiparticle mechanism, reinforcing the credibility of the calculated Equation of State. Finally, the quasiparticle model extension improves PNJL from a descriptive tool to a more qualitative phenomenological approach, enabling an improved description of the strong interacting quark-gluon plasma.

### [47] [Hard-Region Fermion Self-Energy and Fermion--Photon Vertex in Thermal QED through Two Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27137)
*Ali Hataei*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统计算了质量零温度QED中一阶次领头功率和二阶领头功率下的硬区费米子自能和费米子-光子顶点，验证了Ward-Takahashi恒等式和轴矢横向性，发现硬区自能修正对费米子阻尼率无有限贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在热场QED中，软动量展开下的硬区贡献对于理解质量移动、包含率和有效拉格朗日量的构造至关重要，但此前缺乏系统的高阶和次领头阶计算与分析。

Method: 采用一般协变$R_ξ$规范，计算一阶次领头功率（NLP）和二阶领头功率（LP）的硬区贡献；包含零温抵消项进行重整化；将振幅分解为独立统计扇区和规范扇区，逐扇区验证WTI和轴矢横向性；分析对称性、厄米性和选择定则。

Result: 轴矢部分横向于光子动量；软展开的选择定则为：贡献仅在$r+N+1$为偶数时非零；规范扇区在二阶分为混合度量-纵向和完全纵向扇区，后者在LP消失而在NLP重现；硬区自能修正不产生费米子阻尼率的有限贡献。

Conclusion: 本文为热QED中费米子质量移动、包含率以及次领头阶费米子有效拉格朗日量的构造提供了完整的硬区输入。

Abstract: In massless thermal QED in a general covariant $R_ξ$ gauge, we compute hard-region contributions to the fermion self-energy and the off-shell fermion--photon vertex at one-loop next-to-leading power and two-loop leading power in the soft-momentum expansion. The zero-temperature counterterms are also included to renormalize these hard amplitudes. Chiral invariance restricts the off-shell two-fermion--$N$-photon vertex to vector ($γ_μ$) and axial-vector ($γ_μγ_5$) Dirac structures. The vector part is constrained by the Ward--Takahashi identity (WTI), while the axial part is transverse to the photon momentum. The symmetries and hermiticity of the theory impose definite constraints -- including reality, momentum reversal, and fermion-leg exchange properties -- which lead to selection rules in the soft expansion: a contribution at power $r$ can be nonzero only when $r+N+1$ is even, with $N=0$ for the self-energy. At the integrand level, we decompose the amplitudes into independent statistical and gauge sectors, and verify the WTI and axial transversality sector by sector. Notably, the gauge-dependent sectors split into mixed metric--longitudinal and fully longitudinal sectors at two loops. The latter vanishes at leading power and reappears at next-to-leading power while satisfying the constraints. We show that these hard-region self-energy corrections do not generate a finite contribution to the fermion damping rate. These results provide hard-region input for mass shifts and inclusive rates, as well as for the construction of the next-to-leading-order fermionic effective Lagrangian.

The correlations between the spin states of the $q\bar{q}$ pair produced in the reaction are described by a joint spin density matrix. The spin correlations are propagated along the string fragmentation chain by using the rules of the string+${}^3P_0$ model and are implemented for the production of pseudoscalar and vector mesons. The new version of the package can be used to simulate spin effects in $e^+e^-$ annihilation like the Collins and the Artru-Collins asymmetries. It can also be applied to the study of other spin effects in hadronization predicted by the string+${}^3P_0$ model with a user-defined joint spin density matrix of the $q\bar{q}$ pair. To showcase the usage of the package the polar angle dependence of the Collins asymmetries for back-to-back pions is studied and compared with the available data.

### [49] [Coherent collective response in many-qubit systems for dark matter detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26736)
*Ryuichiro Kitano,Ryoto Takai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用N个叠加态（|0⟩+|1⟩）^⊗N的Ramsey型干涉仪阵列来探测波状暗物质。该方法无需纠缠态，信噪比正比于√N α，灵敏度δα~1/√N。使用离子阱量子比特，N≥10^6时灵敏度可超越现有实验、天体物理和宇宙学限制。该方法也适用于高频引力波探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗物质探测方案中，基于Rabi型跃迁的方案需要高度纠缠的N个量子比特才能实现δα~1/√N的灵敏度缩放，而纠缠态在大规模系统中制备和维持极为困难。作者希望设计一种无需纠缠态但同样能实现量子增强灵敏度的暗物质探测方案。

Method: 利用N个处于叠加态(|0⟩+|1⟩)^⊗N的量子比特作为Ramsey型干涉仪阵列。暗物质波诱导相干量子比特跃迁后，通过测量0和1探测概率的不平衡量作为信号。信噪比正比于√N α。在暗物质德布罗意波长内简单放置大量量子比特即可实现大N，无需纠缠态。

Result: 在基于离子阱量子比特的线性Paul阱中，当N≥10^6时，投影灵敏度可匹配或超越现有实验室约束、天体物理和宇宙学界限。该方法同样可应用于高频引力波探测。

Conclusion: 该Ramsey型干涉仪阵列框架为波状暗物质探测提供了一种无需纠缠态的量子增强方案，原则上适用于其他量子传感平台。

Abstract: We propose an array of the Ramsey-type interferometers using $N$ superposition states, $(|0\rangle+ |1\rangle)^{\otimes N}$, as a sensor to detect wave-like dark matter. After the exposure to the dark matter wave, which induces the coherent qubit transitions, the signal is the imbalance between the probabilities of detecting 0 and 1. The signal-to-noise ratio in this scheme is proportional to $\sqrt{N} α$, where $α$ is the coupling of dark matter to the qubits, and thus the sensitivity to the coupling scales as $δα\sim 1 / \sqrt{N}$. For comparison, in the detection scheme based on the Rabi-type transition, $|0\rangle \to |1\rangle$, this scaling is achieved only when highly entangled $N$ qubits are used. Since the Ramsey-type measurement does not require entangled states, one can consider much larger $N$ by simply placing a large number of qubits within the de Broglie wavelength of the dark matter. We demonstrate that, using trapped-ion qubits in a linear Paul trap as the sensor, the projected sensitivity to the coupling matches or surpasses existing laboratory, astrophysical, and cosmological bounds for $N \gtrsim 10^6$. We also evaluate its sensitivity to high-frequency gravitational waves. Our general framework should, in principle, be useful for other quantum sensing platforms.

### [50] [A fidelity metric for quantum annealing benchmarked by extreme scaling quantum Monte-Carlo simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26233)
*Gabriel Gouraud,Miha Srdinsek,Xavier Waintal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于量子退火过程质量评估的保真度度量（类似门型量子计算机的每门保真度），即退火器状态方程的精度ε，并通过两种模拟量子退火方法（变分量子蒙特卡洛和格林函数量子蒙特卡洛）在里德伯原子系统中计算了基准值，分别达到了10^-2-10^-3（最多1亿原子）和10^-4（最多10万原子）的精度，远超当前实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子退火器性能评估过度依赖于特定优化问题的解决效果和与经典算法的对比，这种评估方法本质上是脆弱的，缺乏一个能够衡量退火过程本身质量的通用度量。

Method: 提出量子退火版本的"每门保真度"度量——退火器状态方程的精度ε；使用两种模拟量子退火技术：1）基于热退火启发的变分量子蒙特卡洛（VMC）；2）基于格林函数的量子蒙特卡洛（GFQMC）。

Result: VMC方法达到ε~10^-2-10^-3精度，可处理最多1亿个原子（单CPU）；GFQMC方法达到ε~10^-4精度，可处理最多10万个原子；两种方法在精度和规模上均远超当前里德伯原子量子退火实验平台数个数量级。

Conclusion: 该度量对未来的量子退火硬件提出了严格的约束条件，即实验平台需要在精度和规模上达到或超越这些经典模拟方法的基准值才能证明量子优势。

Abstract: Quantum annealers are supposed to follow adiabatically the ground state of a system as its Hamiltonian slowly interpolates between a trivial phase and a non-trivial one; the non-trivial ground state being the solution to an optimization problem. Overwhelmingly, their performances are measured in terms of how well or fast the optimization problem is solved. While pragmatic, this approach is inherently brittle as it strongly depends on the problem considered and the classical algorithm used as the reference benchmark. Here, we propose a quantity that not only measures the end result but also the quality of the actual quantum annealing process itself. Our metric is the quantum annealing counterpart of the fidelity-per gate of gate-based quantum computers. It takes the form of an accuracy $ε$ for the equation of state of the annealer. We calculate benchmark values of $ε$ using two variants of the simulated quantum annealing technique for Rydberg atoms systems. Our first approach uses variational quantum Monte-Carlo with an ansatz inspired by thermal annealing. It suggests that within $ε\sim 10^{-2}-10^{-3}$, a quantum annealer is indistinguishable from its thermal classical counterpart. Critically, we could reach this precision up to $100,000,000$ atoms on a single CPU. Our second approach (based on Green function quantum Monte-Carlo) reaches accuracies around $ε\sim 10^{-4}$ and we have run it up to $100,000$ atoms. These results outperform current Rydberg atom quantum annealing experimental platforms in both precision and size by orders of magnitude and put severe constraints for future hardware.

</details>


### [51] [Dissipative Quantum Multiplicative Weights with Sampling Feedback: A Classically Hard Primitive Realized via Engineered Open-System Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26162)
*Agung Trisetyarso,Lenny Putri Yulianti,Kridanto Surendro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出DQMW-Sample，一种利用工程化开放量子系统动力学制备吉布斯态以提供在线学习反馈的原语。通过构建经典无法高效模拟的Davies型耗散器，实现了量子与经典学习者在在线学习中计算优势的分离，并证明了噪声下的亚线性遗憾界。在IBM Heron r2处理器上完成了初步硬件验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将恒温吉布斯采样的计算困难性转化为可物理实现的在线学习原语，从复杂性理论角度证明量子在线学习相对于经典学习者的计算优势，并探索其与近期超导硬件的兼容性。

Method: 提出DQMW-Sample原语，通过工程化Davies型耗散器（其每轮反馈无法被经典高效模拟）来制备吉布斯态；设计平衡耗散调度以抑制硬件噪声；利用谱间隙收缩噪声诱导的遗憾；构造特定实例使经典学习器只能达到常数平均遗憾。

Result: DQMW-Sample实现了渐近次线性遗憾，而所有高效经典学习器在构造的实例上遭受常数平均遗憾（计算分离）；在平衡耗散调度下实现噪声诱导的亚线性遗憾；整个T轮反馈过程的经典模拟将导致多项式谱系坍缩；在IBM Heron r2处理器上完成了初始硬件表征。

Conclusion: DQMW-Sample为在线学习中实现计算优势提供了基于复杂性理论且兼容近期超导硬件的具体路线。

Abstract: We introduce \emph{Dissipative Quantum Multiplicative Weights with Sampling Feedback} (DQMW-Sample), an online-learning primitive in which engineered open quantum-system dynamics prepare a Gibbs state whose computational-basis measurement supplies the loss feedback. The central conceptual contribution is to lift the computational hardness of constant-temperature Gibbs sampling into a physically realizable online-learning primitive. By engineering a Davies-type dissipator whose per-round feedback cannot be efficiently simulated classically, we obtain a learning-theoretic separation in which DQMW-Sample achieves asymptotically sublinear regret while every efficient classical learner suffers constant average regret on a suitably constructed instance. We further prove that the spectral gap of the engineered dissipator contracts hardware noise, yielding sublinear noise-induced regret under a balanced dissipation schedule, and we strengthen the single-round hardness to the full adaptive interaction: an efficient classical simulator of the entire $T$-round feedback process would collapse the polynomial hierarchy. We state the required realizability assumption in explicit form and report an initial hardware characterization on the IBM Heron~r2 processor. These results position DQMW-Sample as a concrete route toward computational advantage in online learning that is grounded in complexity theory and compatible with near-term superconducting hardware.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合态拓扑相的手性缺乏严格的数学-物理对应，纯态中成熟的手性诊断方案在混合态中失效，需要建立全新的诊断框架。

Method: 从已知无错误母态出发，利用退相干构造混合态拓扑相，提出两种基于相对熵的度量来诊断手性，其中一种可进一步提取手性中心荷。

Abstract: What does it mean for a mixed-state topological phase to be chiral? Mathematically, chirality can be sharply characterized through the symmetry algebra of the mixed state. Physically, however, the question is far more subtle. In pure states, chirality in topological phase is tied to a web of familiar diagnostics, involving bulk-boundary correspondence, a gapless entanglement spectrum, a nontrivial modular commutator, and a quantized thermal Hall response. We show that none of these diagnostics remain reliable in mixed states. Instead, for decohered topological phases with a known error-free parent state, we propose two relative-entropy-based measures that can diagnose chirality, with one of them further extracting the chiral central charge. Our results emphasize how mixed-state topology demands intrinsically new diagnostics beyond direct analogues of pure-state probes.

### [53] [Criterion for qubit-assisted quantum metrology approaching Heisenberg scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26167)
*Peng Chen,Jun Jing*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了与辅助量子比特耦合的探针系统的计量精度，发现探针-量子比特耦合仅沿一或两个方向是有效动力学生成元达到海森堡极限的充分条件。在玻色子探针中，位移估计的量子Fisher信息与探针平均激发数成正比，表明可通过升温增强量子计量灵敏度；在自旋系综探针中，旋转相位和磁场估计的QFI均与探针自旋数呈二次依赖关系，即使自旋系综处于有限温度状态（远非压缩态或GHZ态等资源态），QFI仍可展现海森堡标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究与辅助量子比特耦合的探针系统在量子计量中的精度极限，特别是确定达到海森堡极限的充分条件，并检验该条件在玻色子和自旋系综两种不同系统中的有效性。

Method: 通过分析探针-量子比特耦合方向（仅一维或二维）对有效动力学生成元的约束，推导出量子Fisher信息与初始态有效生成元均方期望值的关系，并在玻色子探针（位移估计）和自旋系综探针（旋转相位及磁场估计）两个系统中验证该判据。

Result: 玻色子探针的QFI正比于平均激发数，温度升高可增强灵敏度；自旋系综探针的QFI与自旋数呈二次关系，即使在有限温度非资源态下仍可实现海森堡标度。

Conclusion: 探针-量子比特耦合方向限制是达到海森堡极限的充分条件，且在热态等非传统资源态下仍可维持海森堡标度行为，拓展了量子计量学的资源范畴。

Abstract: We study in this work the metrology precision of a probe system coupled to an ancillary qubit. Restricting the probe-qubit coupling along only one or two directions is found to be a sufficient criterion for the effective dynamical generator to achieve the Heisenberg limit in precision. Under the criterion, the quantum Fisher information (QFI) about the to-be-estimated parameter becomes the expectation value of mean square of the effective generator with respect to the initial state of the composite system. Our criterion is justified in two distinct systems. For a bosonic probe, QFI about the displacement estimation is found to be proportional to the mean excitation number of probe. It renders a counterintuitive result that quantum metrology sensitivity can be enhanced by increasing the temperature of the probe system. For a spin-ensemble probe, QFI about both rotation-phase and magnetic-field estimation exhibit a quadratic dependence on the probe-spin number. It is found that even when the spin-ensemble is prepared as a finite-temperature state, faraway from the so-called resource states, e.g., the squeezed state or the Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger state, QFI can still manifest a Heisenberg scaling behavior.

</details>


### [54] [Optimal observables for quantum-enhanced sensing and applications in a Floquet time crystal sensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26248)

Abstract: In this work, we discuss how to determine and implement feasible optimal observables for a metrology protocol that saturates the quantum Fisher information (QFI) bound. In particular, we focus our study on a simple protocol, namely the method of moments (MoM). We first demonstrate that the symmetric logarithmic derivative (SLD) operator, a Hermitian observable, once implemented in the MoM, saturates the QFI bound. However, the SLD is generally too complex and typically non-local, rendering its direct experimental realization unfeasible. To overcome this limitation, we explore its structure in a specific sensing model - a Floquet time crystal (FTC) acting as an ac field sensor - and show that the SLD can be approximated by substantially simpler observables, such as the bare spin magnetization or a parity observable, for different relevant initial state preparations. We further corroborate our theoretical predictions in a nuclear magnetic resonance system operating as an FTC sensor, employing experimentally motivated parameters to simulate its performance in a state-of-the-art implementation. In general, our results establish a practical route toward near-optimal metrology in FTC sensors, where the inaccessible SLD operator can be replaced by simpler observables while retaining quantum-enhanced sensitivity.

Our results highlight that accurate and interpretable learning can emerge from autonomous stochastic dynamics, and establish thermodynamic computation as a viable framework for physical machine learning.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: All maximally entangled two-qubit states violate local realism with the same probability under uniformly random projective measurements, yet they need not behave identically in randomized Bell tests. We show that when measurement settings are exchanged between the parties in sequential Bell experiments, permutation symmetry of the shared state determines the statistical relation between the two realizations. Permutationally invariant states yield identical nonlocality outcomes in both experiments, whereas asymmetric states can violate local realism in one realization but not in the other. This distinction leads to two operational consequences. First, it enables the detection of correlations between the measurement choices of Alice and Bob through the joint violation statistics. Second, in Bell tests with finite measurement pools, asymmetric maximally entangled states can significantly increase the probability of observing nonlocality without requiring additional resources. Our results identify permutation asymmetry as a useful feature in randomized Bell experiments and highlight a new role of symmetry in quantum nonlocality.
