Abstract: We revisit the quantum annealing problem in the non-Hermitian transverse-field Ising model. We determine, both analytically and numerically, the intrinsic transition probabilities and the resulting defect density. Our results reveal that, unlike the Hermitian case where defect production is dominated by modes near the gap-closing point, the non-Hermitian dynamics involve significant contributions from broad momentum sectors. We find that, depending on the dissipation strength, the defect density exhibits standard Kibble-Zurek scaling, anti-Kibble-Zurek behavior, and a suppression faster than the Kibble-Zurek prediction. We demonstrate that these deviations from the standard Kibble-Zurek scaling can be understood in terms of the underlying excitation probabilities. Specifically, the fast decay of the defect density originates from a vanishing excitation probability spanning a range of annealing times across all allowed modes, even at the gap-closing points. In contrast, the anti-Kibble-Zurek behavior arises from supplementary excitations facilitated by dissipation over a broad range of allowed modes, particularly those situated away from the gap-closing region.

### [61] [From Approximate Floquet Engineering to Full Floquet Theory: Coherent Control of Chiral Spin Systems in Spintronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27183)
*Andrea Simion,Claudiu Filip,Coriolan Tiusan*

Abstract: Coherent control of interacting spin systems under time-periodic driving is a central challenge in spin-based quantum technologies. Here we demonstrate the applicability of a full Floquet-space formalism, adapted from Nuclear Magnetic Resonance (NMR) methodologies, to model the dynamics of driven coupled electron spins in the presence of a static magnetic field B0 and a transverse oscillating field B1. The framework explicitly includes isotropic exchange coupling J and the chiral Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya antisymmetric exchange interaction (DMI), and its numerical convergence is systematically validated with respect to Fourier-space truncation. In the non-interacting limit, the expected driven-spin dynamics is recovered, with the oscillation periodicity governed by B1. Exchange coupling alone does not modify the collective spin expectation values under the chosen initial condition, consistent with symmetry considerations. In contrast, increasing DMI generates a finite expectation value of Sy, suppresses the expectation value of Sz, and produces tilted, elliptical Bloch-sphere trajectories, reflecting the emergence of chiral spin-spin correlations. These effects are pronounced for open boundary conditions, while remaining nearly negligible in the periodic boundary case. When exchange coupling and DMI coexist, the dynamics becomes strongly perturbed and multi-frequency in nature. Together, these results demonstrate that full Floquet-space modeling provides a robust and predictive framework for analyzing and engineering coherent dynamics in driven interacting spin systems beyond simple coherent-rotation regimes.

Method: 引入合适的Liouville超算符的算符表示，将动力学表述为厄密算符的闭合代数；推导递推关系以高效构造任意维度系统的代数基；所有模型依赖信息通过单一系数集进入框架。

Abstract: We investigate the algebraic structure underlying the Lindblad equation for finite-dimensional open quantum systems. By introducing a suitable operator representation of the Liouville superoperator, we show that the dynamics can be formulated in terms of a closed algebra of Hermitian operators that is independent of the particular physical model. This formulation reveals that dissipative dynamics requires a substantially richer algebraic structure than purely unitary evolution, thereby providing a clear characterization of the additional complexity introduced by the Lindbladian. The resulting framework naturally leads to parametrizations of the dynamical map and to differential equations governing its evolution. We further derive recursion relations that enable the efficient construction of the algebra for systems of increasing dimension. Because the algebraic basis is universal, while all model-dependent information enters through a single set of coefficients, the proposed approach significantly reduces the computational cost of constructing the Liouville superoperator compared with direct methods. To facilitate the implementation of the method, we provide a Mathematica notebook containing a one-qubit example that can be systematically extended to an arbitrary number of qubits. The proposed framework therefore provides both a general mathematical description of finite-dimensional Lindblad dynamics and a practical foundation for efficient analytical and numerical implementations.

Abstract: Device-independent quantum key distribution (DI-QKD) offers security with the smallest possible set of assumptions about the experimental setup. The challenge posed by its implementation could be tackled using routed Bell tests with entanglement swapping, or distant Bell state measurement (BSM) units. However, practical distances still require local tests with close-to-ideal violations. We propose a DI-QKD protocol based on multiple sources and measurement devices where, in each round, routed tests are performed on randomly selected local devices. The violation of local Bell tests is checked even when a successful BSM projection is achieved. By requiring that such conditional tests remain consistent with the overall one, we achieve improvements in the critical detection efficiencies of about $4-12\%$ for high visibilities. Our approach enables long-distance DI-QKD, with access to highly efficient loophole-free routing setups, and multiple local tests (possibly imperfect) with very high local detection efficiencies. Finally, we extend the concept of routing to dimension witnesses, where qubit-bounded sources send states to the BSM. ### [69] [Quantum Fast-Forwarding Beyond Reversibility: The $α$-Perturbed $n$-Cycle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26584)
*Avah Banerjee,Asim Sharma,Sooraj Sooman*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究量子快进（QFF）能否从可逆马尔可夫链扩展到非可逆情形。以α扰动的n-环马尔可夫链为例，发现非可逆时特征值离开[-1,1]区间，导致精确的Chebyshev基QFF无法直接推广。但通过截断Chebyshev和LCU技术，仍可获得有限时间近似，其多项式度数τ=O(|α|t+√(t log(t/η)))，仅在|α|=O(t^{-1/2})的微扰区恢复O(√t)的可逆加速行为，表明不可逆性会退化解的加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究量子快进框架能否从可逆马尔可夫链扩展到非可逆动力学，并量化非可逆性对量子加速效果的影响。

Method: 以α扰动的n-环马尔可夫链为模型（保持循环结构但引入可控非可逆性），分析特征值变化；利用截断Chebyshev多项式和LCU（线性组合酉算子）技术实现有限时间近似。

Result: 非可逆情形（α≠0）下特征值离开[-1,1]区间，T_m(P_α)无法均匀有界，精确Chebyshev基QFF无法直接推广；通过近似方法得到度数τ=O(|α|t+√(t log(t/η)))的多项式，仅在|α|=O(t^{-1/2})时可恢复O(√t)的加速。

Conclusion: 精确的Chebyshev基QFF不能直接扩展到非可逆情形，但存在一个近可逆的微扰区（|α|=O(t^{-1/2})）内QFF仍有效，且不可逆性会量化地退化解的加速效果。

Abstract: Quantum fast-forwarding (QFF) is usually formulated for reversible Markov chains, where the projected quantum walk evolution is exactly governed by Chebyshev polynomials of a Hermitian discriminant matrix. We study whether this framework can be extended to nonreversible dynamics for an $α$-perturbed $n$-cycle Markov chain, which preserves circulant structure while introducing controlled irreversibility.
  We show that the nonreversible case has a fundamental obstruction: for $α\neq 0$, the eigenvalues of $P_α$ leave the interval $[-1,1]$, so $T_m(P_α)$ is not uniformly bounded and cannot arise as an exact unitary compression for all times. Thus, exact Chebyshev-based QFF does not extend directly beyond reversibility.
  Nevertheless, we obtain a finite-time approximation result using truncated Chebyshev and LCU techniques. The evolution $P_α^t$ can be approximated with degree $τ=O\left(|α|t+\sqrt{t\log(t/η)}\right),$ which recovers the reversible $O(\sqrt t)$ behavior only in the perturbative regime $|α|=O(t^{-1/2})$. This identifies a nearly reversible regime where QFF survives perturbatively and quantifies how irreversibility degrades the speedup.

It enables the realization of a non-Hermitian Hamiltonian of interest using a Hermitian quadratic bosonic system. Unlike previous dissipation-driven non-Hermitian mechanisms, effective parity-time ($\mathcal{PT}$) symmetry arises purely from squeezing and exchanges gainy and lossy eigenmodes. We identify non-Hermiticity of an anomalous superradiant phase for strong spins squeezing, exhibiting spontaneous breaking of the unique $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry beyond $Z_2$ symmetries. Such exotic phase exhibits a complex excitation spectrum and undergoes a dynamical phase transition to a conventional superradiant phase at an exceptional point. An artificial magnetic field combined with the broken Hermiticity yields nonreciprocal dynamics with striking quantum amplification, exhibiting unidirectional enhanced transmission. Our Hermitian light-matter system offers an alternative pathway to exotic non-Hermitian physics and nonreciprocal quantum amplification.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对无跳跃 regime 下由非厄米有效哈密顿量描述的三能级驱动系统，在双正交框架下设计定制复脉冲，确保计算子空间演化在最终时刻精确闭合，实现非幺正动力学下的任意单量子比特全息门，且无需在正交补空间中实现循环演化。

Result: 该方法将裸本征态的衰变和退相干预先纳入脉冲设计，使得耗散不会降低无跳跃门保真度，相较于现有非厄米处理方案有明显改进。

Conclusion: 所提出的非绝热全息方案能够有效应对现实量子系统中的退相干挑战，为在耗散环境中实现高保真度量子门提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Holonomic quantum computation offers a promising route to robust quantum gates, but decoherence remains a central obstacle in realistic implementations. Here we develop a nonadiabatic holonomic scheme for a driven three-level system in the no-jump regime described by an effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian. Within a biorthogonal framework, tailored complex pulses enforce exact closure of the computational-subspace evolution at the final time despite the underlying nonunitary dynamics, enabling arbitrary single-qubit holonomic gates without requiring cyclic evolution in its orthogonal complement. In contrast to existing non-Hermitian treatments, which either neglect the overall exponential prefactor or, in adiabatic settings, include dissipation only on the auxiliary excited level, our scheme incorporates decay and dephasing of all bare eigenstates directly into the pulse design, so that dissipation does not reduce the no-jump gate fidelity.

Abstract: Graphs provide a natural language for relational data in chemistry, biology and optimisation. Graph neural networks (GNNs) have driven much of the recent progress in learning from such data through message passing, a single primitive that generalises convolution and attention. Quantum counterparts have been proposed, but with limited connection to message passing and few guarantees on performance or scalability. More broadly, the trainability of variational quantum circuits is a recognised bottleneck for their wide applicability, and pre-training has emerged as one way to address it. Yet for a quantum model to be useful, it must offer expressivity guarantees along with demonstrable scalability. Here we show how a quantum graph neural network can be built to perform message passing, to be permutation equivariant, and to sit at a chosen level of the Weisfeiler-Leman hierarchy, the standard measure of how finely a model can tell graphs apart. We validate the framework in large-scale simulations of up to 56 qubits across three datasets, on synthetic graphs that ordinary message passing cannot separate, on molecular property prediction, and on the travelling salesperson problem. Our framework opens a path for near-term quantum algorithms with theoretical guarantees and practical scalability, bringing the principles of graph learning into quantum circuit design.

Here we develop a numerical framework for multi-tone gate synthesis that directly searches for control fields satisfying these competing requirements. Abstract: Conventional stellar interferometry reconstructs incoherent sources from pairwise mutual coherences between telescopes. Are such pairwise measurements sufficient for quantum-limited subdiffraction imaging with a telescope array? We show that for generic image-moment estimation, they are not. We consider weak incoherent light from a generic extended source observed by an array of telescopes, each supporting a single optical mode. For an N-telescope array, we derive the quantum Fisher information (QFI) scaling of image moments up to the cutoff 2N-2 and prove that arbitrary measurements restricted to telescope pairs attain the full-array QFI scaling only up to second order. Thus, estimating higher-order moments at the quantum limit requires genuinely multi-telescope interference. Inspired by spatial-mode demultiplexing (SPADE) from single-aperture subdiffraction imaging, we construct array-SPADE measurements that attain the optimal QFI scaling up to the finite-array cutoff. Finally, we show that these measurements can, in principle, be embedded in ancilla- and memory-assisted quantum-network architectures for long-baseline telescopy.

### [77] [Self-Sifting quantum key distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27299)
*Saman Sarshar,Mostafa Annabestani*

TL;DR: 提出了一种新型两向量子密钥分发协议，基于最大纠缠Bell态和 scrambling 算子安全机制，所有筛选和窃听检测由Bob在量子通信完成后执行，控制模式永不公开，传输量子比特不直接编码密钥信息，并可利用通常丢弃的轮次检测窃听者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统两路QKD协议存在控制模式公开宣布导致的安全漏洞，攻击者可根据模式自适应攻击或隐藏在控制模式中；此外，攻击者可能从直接编码密钥信息的传输量子比特中获取信息。本文旨在解决这些问题。

Method: 1) 使用最大纠缠Bell态的单个量子比特作为量子信道；2) 引入基于scrambling算子的新安全机制；3) 所有筛选和窃听检测推迟到量子通信完成后由Bob单方执行；4) 控制模式永不公开；5) 传输量子比特不直接编码密钥信息；6) 利用通常丢弃的轮次进行窃听检测。

Result: 分析表明，对于最一般形式的基于辅助系统的攻击（Eve将辅助系统耦合到传输量子比特以获取密钥信息），该协议能够有效检测。

Conclusion: 该协议通过设计上的创新（延迟检测、控制模式不公开、传输量子比特不编码密钥、利用丢弃轮次检测）从根本上防止了依赖模式自适应的攻击，并限制了从量子信道攻击中可提取的信息量。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce a novel two-way quantum key distribution (QKD) protocol in which the sender (Alice) and receiver (Bob) employ one qubit of a maximally entangled Bell state as the quantum channel for key exchange. The protocol incorporates a new security mechanism based on a scrambling operator. Unlike conventional two-way QKD protocols, all sifting operations and eavesdropper detection procedures are postponed until the completion of the quantum communication stage and are performed exclusively by Bob. Since the control mode is never publicly announced, attacks that rely on mode-dependent adaptations or attempt to remain hidden within the control mode are inherently prevented. Furthermore, the traveling qubit does not directly encode key information, substantially limiting the information that can be extracted from attacks targeting the quantum channel alone. An additional distinctive feature of the protocol is that rounds that would ordinarily be discarded can instead be utilized to detect the presence of an eavesdropper. We analyze a broad class of ancilla-based attacks, in which an eavesdropper couples an ancillary system to the transmitted qubit in an attempt to gain information about the key, and show that such attacks are detectable in their most general form.

### [78] [Cultivating logical catalysts for fault-tolerant dyadic phase rotations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27358)
*Yichen Xu,Xiao Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种表面码催化协议，用于制备可重复使用的逻辑催化剂态，通过相位反冲实现精确的精细二进相位门 $Z^{2^{-b}}$。催化剂是高周期 Clifford 电路 $U$ 的本征态，直接构建在 $O(2^b)$ 个逻辑量子比特上。每次调用通过受控-$U$ 门实现目标相位，消除了 Clifford+$T$ 合成近似误差，并将在线非 Clifford 深度与目标逻辑精度解耦。以 $\sqrt{T}=Z^{1/8}$ 为例，催化剂为九量子比特砖墙 Clifford 电路，受控-$U$ 包含八个受控-CNOT。从九个距离三的旋转表面码块开始，通过逻辑-$U$ 校验、纠错提取和后选择、码生长及互补间隙解码来培养催化剂。由于相位读出的固有容错性，单次验证轮次即可达到领先的纠错缩放，而单量子比特魔法态需要重复逻辑校验。混合张量网络和稳定子模拟显示，在物理错误率 $p=10^{-3}$ 下，后选择催化剂可生长至距离七的旋转表面码块，逻辑泄漏率约 $10^{-6}$，约需七次预期尝试，更强的后选择可进一步压制。与现有协议相比，该方法用离线、相位特定的催化剂培养换取了精确性、可重用性和受限横向门集代码中固定精细二进相的常数深度在线实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Clifford+$T$ 门集实现非 Clifford 门需要近似合成，引入近似误差且在线深度随精度增长。本文旨在设计一种可重复使用的逻辑催化剂态，通过相位反冲精确实现精细二进相位门，消除近似误差并实现与精度无关的常数深度在线实现。

Method: 提出表面码催化协议：1) 构建高周期 Clifford 电路 $U$ 的本征态作为催化剂，支持在 $O(2^b)$ 逻辑量子比特上直接构造；2) 通过受控-$U$ 门实现相位反冲；3) 使用逻辑-$U$ 校验、纠错提取和后选择、码生长、互补间隙解码来培养催化剂；4) 单次验证轮次利用相位读出的固有容错性。

Result: 以 $\sqrt{T}=Z^{1/8}$ 为演示，催化剂为九量子比特砖墙 Clifford 电路，受控-$U$ 仅含八个受控-CNOT。混合张量网络和稳定子模拟显示，物理错误率 $p=10^{-3}$ 下，后选择催化剂可生长至距离七的旋转表面码块，逻辑泄漏率 $\sim 10^{-6}$，约需七次预期尝试。

Conclusion: 该方法用离线、相位特定的催化剂培养换取了精确性、可重用性和常数深度在线实现，适用于受限横向门集代码中固定精细二进相位的实现，相比单量子比特魔法态培养具有更高效的纠错缩放。

Abstract: We introduce a surface-code cultivation protocol for reusable logical catalyst states that implement exact fine dyadic phase gates $Z^{2^{-b}}$ by phase kickback. The catalyst is an eigenstate of a high-period Clifford circuit $U$, with a direct construction supported on $O(2^b)$ logical qubits. Once cultivated, each invocation implements the target phase through a controlled-$U$ gadget, removing Clifford+$T$ synthesis approximation error from the online gate and making the online non-Clifford depth independent of the target logical accuracy. As a concrete demonstration, we construct a catalyst for $\sqrt{T}=Z^{1/8}$, where $U$ is a nine-qubit brickwork Clifford circuit and controlled-$U$ consists of eight controlled-CNOTs. Starting from nine distance-three rotated-surface-code blocks, we cultivate the catalyst through logical-$U$ checks, syndrome extraction and postselection, code growth, and complementary-gap decoding. Due to the intrinsic fault tolerance of the phase read-out, a \emph{single} verification round already reaches the leading error-corrected scaling, in contrast to the repeated logical checks required when cultivating single-qubit magic states. A hybrid tensor-network and stabilizer simulation shows that, at physical error rate $p=10^{-3}$, the postselected catalyst can be grown to distance-seven rotated-surface-code blocks with logical leakage rate $\sim 10^{-6}$ using around seven expected attempts, and can be suppressed further with stronger postselection. Compared with existing protocols, our approach trades offline, phase-specific catalyst cultivation for exactness, reusability, and constant-depth online implementation of fixed fine dyadic phases in codes with restricted transversal gate sets.

</details>

Abstract: Computing the structure of the Hochschild (co)homology and the cyclic homology of an algebra can be hard work, but Etingof and Eu showed that it can be done surprisingly easily for preprojective algebras of ADE Dynkin type, at least if one only wants to know the graded vector space structure of each Hochschild cohomology group. Their method is based on exploiting strong structural features of such a preprojective algebra via a graded Euler characteristic that can computed using the algebra's graded Cartan matrix. In this paper, we present a generalization of the method used by Etingof and Eu to higher preprojective algebras. We also apply our generalization to the higher preprojective algebras of the 2-representation finite algebras that arise as tensor products of representation finite hereditary algebras of type A. For this, it turns out to be enough to know the graded vector space structure of the center and the zeroth Hochschild homology to be able to deduce the graded vector space structure of the Hochschild (co)homology and the cyclic homology in all other degrees.

### [81] [Brick infinite algebras admit infinitely many non-$τ$-rigid bricks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27063)
*Kaveh Mousavand,Charles Paquette*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文证明：若一个有限维代数A的所有except有限多个砖模都是τ-刚性的，则A是砖有限的。等价地，任何砖无限代数都有无限多个非τ-刚性的砖模。这一结果验证了开猜想的一个弱版本，并解决了此前仅对E-驯顺代数已知的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 砖模与τ-刚性模之间存在基础性相互作用，受此启发，作者希望在没有驯顺性假设的一般情形下，证明"几乎所有砖模都是τ-刚性"蕴含"砖有限性"，从而验证一个关于"几乎所有砖模都是刚性的则代数砖有限"这一开猜想的弱版本，并推进与第二砖-Brauer-Thrall猜想相关的一系列挑战性问题。

Method: 利用砖模与τ-刚性模之间的基础性相互作用关系，在一般有限维代数（代数闭域上）上通过纯代数的论证方式来证明结论，无需驯顺性假设。

Result: 在完全一般性下证明了：如果代数A的所有except有限多个砖模都是τ-刚性的，则A是砖有限的。等价地，任何砖无限代数都拥有无限多个非τ-刚性的砖模。由于τ-刚性蕴含刚性，这验证了开猜想的一个弱版本。同时，该结果在没有驯顺性假设的情形下解决了此前仅对E-驯顺代数已知的问题。

Conclusion: 该工作强化了此前的一些结果，推进了与第二砖-Brauer-Thrall猜想相关的一系列挑战性问题的研究，在没有驯顺性假设的一般情形下回答了此前仅对E-驯顺代数成立的问题。

Abstract: Let $A$ be a finite dimensional algebra over an algebraically closed field. Motivated by some foundational interactions between bricks and $τ$-rigid modules, we prove, in full generality, that if all but finitely many bricks of the algebra $A$ are $τ$-rigid, then $A$ is brick-finite. Equivalently, any brick-infinite algebra admits infinitely many bricks which are not $τ$-rigid. Because $τ$-rigidity implies rigidity, our result verifies a weaker version of an open conjecture which states that if (almost) all bricks over $A$ are rigid, then $A$ should be brick-finite. In retrospect, this work strengthens some previous results and contributes to the recent studies of a series of challenging problems, all tied to the $2$nd brick-Brauer-Thrall conjecture. More specifically, without any tameness assumption, we settle a question that was previously known only for $E$-tame algebras.

</details>

*Rekha Biswal,Patrick Polo*

TL;DR: 本文研究了对称化Kac-Moody代数$mathfrak{g}$的不可约可积模$L(ρ)$的晶体$B(ρ)$，针对Dynkin图中仅含简单边且无长度≥3环路的子图$I$，构造了依赖于根顶点选择的元素$π_{D,I}$，证明了它们是$ρ$-dominant元素，从而为张量积$L(ρ)⊗L(ρ)$提供了新的分支族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对Dynkin子图$I$（仅含简单边、无长度≥3环）的子集$D$，定义$β_D$为对应单根之和；在$λ_{D,I}=2ρ-β_I-β_D$ dominant的条件下，基于每个连通分量根顶点的选择，构造晶体$B(ρ)$中权重为$λ_{D,I}-ρ$的元素$π_{D,I}$。

Abstract: Let $\mathfrak{g}$ be a symmetrizable Kac-Moody algebra over $\mathbb{C}$ and let $L(ρ)$ be the irreducible integrable $\mathfrak{g}$-module with highest weight $ρ$. Let $I$ be a subgraph of the Dynkin diagram of $\mathfrak{g}$ which has only simple bonds and no cycle of length $\geq 3$. For every subset $D$ of $I$, denote by $β_D$ the sum of the simple roots corresponding to $D$. To every $D \subset I$ such that $λ_{D,I} = 2ρ- β_I - β_D$ is dominant, we associate certain elements $π_{D,I}$ of weight $λ_{D,I} {-} ρ$ in the crystal $B(ρ)$, which depend on the choice of a root vertex in each connected component of $I$. Then we prove that our elements are $ρ$-dominant
  elements of $B(ρ)$, hence provide new families of components
  of the tensor product $L(ρ)\otimes L(ρ)$.

The proof combines our general cancellation theorem for complex algebraic varieties with a unique singularity, whose proof relies on the analytic cancellation theorem of Hauser--Müller, with an exponent rigidity theorem for Brieskorn--Pham varieties. Motivation: 理解Noether-Lefschetz除子上光滑四次曲面中曲线的几何性质，特别是其在Hilbert概形中的行为以及Rao函数，以深化对这类特殊曲面中曲线分类和变形理论的认识。

Method: 通过分析四次曲面X中包含一条指定直线L的线性系统，研究其中光滑不可约曲线的存在性；利用Hilbert概形的局部性质验证一般成员的光滑性；运用上同调方法计算Rao函数。

Result: 确定了哪些线性系统包含光滑不可约曲线；证明了大多数类的般成员是预期Hilbert概形的光滑点；计算了X上任意曲线的Rao函数。

Conclusion: 对Noether-Lefschetz除子上光滑四次曲面中的曲线给出了较为完整的分类描述，包括其Hilbert概形的局部结构及上同调不变量。

Abstract: Let $X\subseteq \mathbb{P}^{3}$ be a very general element of the Noether-Lefschetz divisor that parametrizing smooth quartic surfaces containing a line. Let $L\subseteq X$ denote the corresponding line. We study the curves contained in $X$ and analyze their behavior in the Hilbert scheme. We first determine which linear systems contain smooth irreducible curves. For most classes, we verify that the general member is a smooth point of the expected Hilbert scheme. Finally we compute the Rao function of any curve on $X$.

</details>

### [91] [The Ising Model Coupled to 2D Gravity: Critical Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27125)
*Maurice Duits,Nathan Hayford,Seung-Yeop Lee*

Main category: math-ph

Method: 采用双正交多项式族关联的Riemann-Hilbert问题框架，通过最速下降法（steepest-descent analysis）进行分析，在局部参量（local parametrices）构造中处理了新的匹配问题特征。

Conclusion: 严格确认了随机曲面上临界Ising模型收敛到(3,4)拓扑极小模型的结论，为矩阵模型在双标度极限下的行为提供了严格的解析证明。

Abstract: We prove that the differential of the log of the partition function for the $2$-matrix model with quartic interactions converges in a certain double-scaling regime to the differential of the $\boldsymbolτ$-function for the $(3,4)$ string equation. This confirms the convergence of the critical Ising model on random surfaces to the $(3,4)$ topological minimal model, which was stated in the works of Douglas and Shenker, Brézin and Kazakov, and Gross and Migdal. Our analysis is based on a steepest-descent analysis of a Riemann-Hilbert problem associated to a family of biorthogonal polynomials. New features in the matching problem in the construction of local parametrices appear.

### [92] [On Support Cardinality for Discrete Schrödinger Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26149)
*Linjun Li*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究有限d维晶格箱上离散薛定谔方程Dirichlet解的非零支撑集最小大小，证明了一个降维原理：解的最小支撑集大小随维度增加不会减小，并由此在四维空间中得到了近乎最优的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索离散薛定谔方程非平凡解能有多稀疏——即解的非零点数量尽可能少但又不全为零（原点处非零）——这一基础性问题。

Method: 通过建立降维原理（dimension-reduction principle），证明d维空间中的最小支撑集大小不小于d-1维空间中的最小支撑集大小，从而将高维问题归约到低维情形进行分析。

Result: 在四维空间中得到了近乎最优的下界估计，与已知的最佳二维构造仅相差一个对数因子。

Conclusion: 降维原理使得任意低维下界自动推广到高维，为理解高维离散薛定谔方程解的稀疏性提供了有效工具。

Abstract: How sparse can a nontrivial solution of a discrete Schrödinger equation be? In this note we study Dirichlet solutions on a finite $d$-dimensional lattice box, allowing an arbitrary real potential, and measure sparsity by the number of lattice sites at which the solution is nonzero (assuming it is nonzero at the origin). Our main result is a dimension-reduction principle: the minimal possible support size cannot decrease when the dimension increases. Consequently, any lower bound proved in dimension $d-1$ automatically yields the same lower bound in dimension $d$. As an application, we obtain a nearly sharp lower bound in four dimensions, matching the best-known two-dimensional constructions up to a logarithmic factor.

</details>


### [93] [The Colored Hofstadter Butterfly as a Many-Body Quantum Hall Phase Diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26256)
*Giovanna Marcelli,Tadahiro Miyao,Domenico Monaco,Stefan Teufel,Marius Wesle*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于一大类弱相互作用晶格费米子系统，彩色Hofstadter蝴蝶图具有多体解释。通过结合准绝热延拓与与分母无关的磁扰动估计，在任意磁通量下构造出具有局部唯一能隙基态的开放参数区域，并证明了多体能隙标架定理：霍尔电导率在均匀能隙区域内恒定且量子化，满足2πσ^H∈Z，从而证明非相互作用Hofstadter蝴蝶的整数颜色可作为相互作用量子霍尔相的霍尔电导率标签。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非相互作用的Hofstadter蝴蝶图推广到相互作用多体系统，证明其在弱相互作用费米子系统中的多体解释，并验证霍尔电导率的量子化在相互作用下仍然保持。

Method: 结合准绝热延拓（quasi-adiabatic continuation）和与分母无关的磁扰动估计（denominator-independent magnetic perturbation estimates），处理包括不可通约磁通量在内的任意通量情况，无需有限磁单胞假设。

Result: 在三维参数空间（磁场b、化学势μ、相互作用强度λ）中构造了无限大相互作用系统具有局部唯一能隙基态的开放区域；在连通均匀能隙区域上证明了多体能隙标架定理：霍尔电导率恒定且量子化，2πσ^H∈Z。

Conclusion: 非相互作用Hofstadter蝴蝶的整数颜色可作为相互作用量子霍尔相的霍尔电导率标签，证明其在弱相互作用下仍然保持。

Abstract: We prove that the colored Hofstadter butterfly has a many-body interpretation for a broad class of weakly interacting lattice fermion systems. Starting from a spectral gap of a Hofstadter-like one-particle Hamiltonian at arbitrary magnetic flux $b$, we construct an open region in the three-dimensional parameter space $(b,μ,λ)$ of magnetic field, chemical potential, and interaction strength on which the infinite-volume interacting system has locally unique gapped ground states. The construction combines quasi-adiabatic continuation in the interaction strength with denominator-independent magnetic perturbation estimates, and therefore covers both commensurate and incommensurate fluxes, where no finite magnetic unit cell exists. On connected uniformly gapped regions meeting the non-interacting plane $λ=0$, we prove a many-body gap-labeling theorem: the Hall conductivity appearing in the macroscopic Ohm's law is constant and quantized, satisfying $2πσ^{\mathrm{H}}\in\mathbb{Z}$. Thus the integer colors of the non-interacting Hofstadter butterfly persist as Hall-conductivity labels of interacting quantum Hall phases.

Method: 提出度量-辛四括号的构造方法（两个斜对称括号相乘），将其嵌入度量-辛动力学框架，并应用于包含平流量的广义二维准地转上层海洋模型（热准地转模型为其特例）。通过该框架，将不可逆性以可控方式引入系统动力学。

Conclusion: 度量-辛动力学四括号形式为在二维准地转海洋模型中引入满足热力学定律的不可逆性提供了通用且灵活的理论工具，可覆盖从理想化到真实海洋动力学的广泛耗散场景。

Abstract: A general formulation of metriplectic dynamics is presented, where the metriplectic four-bracket is constructed by multiplying two skew-symmetric brackets. The new formulation is then used to introduce irreversibility in a generalized two-dimensional (2D) quasigeostrophic (QG) upper-ocean model involving advected quantities, with the thermal QG model as a special case. By construction, the resulting dynamics ensure the conservation of internal energy and the generation of entropy, in accordance with the first and second laws of thermodynamics. Our metriplectic dynamics formulation allows for a flexible specification of irreversibility, ranging from a type that results in nearly material conservation of potential vorticity to the representation of realistic forcing and dissipation in 2D QG ocean modeling with advected quantities.

*Gerald V. Dunne,Ayssar I. Farah*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了当弱耦合展开的收敛半径为零而强耦合展开的收敛半径为无穷大时（或反之），两者之间存在显式的复苏对偶关系，补充了有限收敛半径或两者均为零半径的情形。通过Airy和Pearcey突变积分、零维φ⁴理论中的Dyson-Schwinger方程以及Gross-Neveu模型中扭结-反扭结晶体的热核迹展开进行了例证。

Method: 利用Airy和Pearcey突变积分的渐近分析，拓展复苏对偶框架，并将其应用于Dyson-Schwinger方程的弱/强耦合展开以及Gross-Neveu模型中热核迹的短/长时间展开。

Result: 成功建立了弱耦合（零收敛半径）与强耦合（无穷大收敛半径）展开之间的显式复苏对偶关系，并通过多个具体实例验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 复苏对偶在展开收敛性质极端不对称（零 vs 无穷大）的情况下仍然成立，为连接不同耦合区域的物理信息提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We show that there is an explicit resurgent duality between weak and strong coupling expansions when one of the expansions has zero radius of convergence and the other has infinite radius of convergence. This complements the situation where the convergent expansion has finite radius of convergence, or when both expansions have zero radius of convergence. We illustrate this phenomenon for the Airy and Pearcey catastrophe integrals, and we apply it to two physical examples: the weak and strong coupling expansions of Dyson-Schwinger equations in zero-dimensional scalar $φ^4$ theories, and the short and long time expansions of the heat kernel trace for the fluctuation operator of the kink-antikink crystal saddle configuration in the Gross-Neveu model.

### [96] [Wave-Particle Decomposition for Kinetic Equations I: Theory and Numerics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26915)
*Chang Liu,Kun Xu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于局部演化时间尺度及其动力学视界的波粒分解（WPD）方法用于动力学松弛方程。通过特征积分解法，将分布函数分解为解析累积的波动分量和纯动力学粒子分量，构建了统一的全努森数波粒系统。该方法在PDE层面定义分区，数值上采用守恒宏微观方法离散，通过形式分析证明了其渐进保持连续极限、稀薄区域一致性及活性动力学自由度的区域自适应缩放，一至三维数值测试验证了精度、多尺度能力和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一气体动力学波粒方法（UGKWP）采用全局时间步分裂，其波粒分区仅在算法层面定义，缺乏PDE层面的连续理论基础。本文旨在建立一种在连续方程层面定义波粒分解的框架，使得分区由局部演化时间尺度与松弛时间之比决定，从而获得更自然的物理意义和更严谨的数学基础。

Method: 利用特征积分解法，将分布函数分解为：1）波动分量——由局域平衡态驱动的解析累积波；2）粒子分量——超出局域影响域（视界）的纯无碰撞输运。在PDE层面构建由守恒律、波动方程和粒子方程组成的统一系统。数值上采用保守的宏微观方法离散，用有限体积更新总守恒变量，结合Navier-Stokes气体动力学波通量与确定性离散纵标（S_N）或蒙特卡洛粒子通量。

Result: 形式分析表明该方法具有渐进保持连续极限特性、稀薄区域一致性，且活性动力学自由度随区域自适应缩放。一维、二维和三维数值测试验证了精度、多尺度能力和计算效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出的波粒分解方法在PDE层面建立了统一的波粒系统，相比UGKWP方法，其分区由局部物理参数决定而非全局时间步分裂，具有更坚实的理论基础和更自然的物理解释。该方法在全努森数范围内有效，兼具精度与效率。

Abstract: This paper presents a wave-particle decomposition (WPD) for kinetic relaxation equations, formulated around a local evolution timescale and its associated kinetic horizon. By leveraging the characteristic integral solution, we decompose the distribution function into an analytically accumulated wave component and a purely kinetic particle component. The latter is defined by the collisionless transport that survives beyond a prescribed local domain of influence, termed the horizon. This continuous formulation yields a unified wave-particle system valid across the entire Knudsen spectrum, comprising a source-free total conservation law, a wave equation, and a particle equation. The wave operator admits a Chapman--Enskog expansion, whose moments yield Euler and Navier--Stokes fluxes with horizon-dependent coefficients, while the particle equation governs the remaining non-equilibrium kinetic transport.
  At the algorithmic level, this system is discretized by a conservative macro-micro method. The total conservative variables are advanced by a finite-volume update using the sum of a Navier--Stokes gas-kinetic wave flux and a particle flux computed by either a deterministic discrete-ordinate $(S_N)$ method or a Monte Carlo representation. Unlike the global time-step splitting in the unified gas-kinetic wave-particle (UGKWP) method, the present partition is defined at the PDE level and governed by the local ratio of evolution timescale to relaxation time. The particle component is therefore a fractional kinetic population generated by the collisionless factor of the integral solution. Formal analysis establishes the asymptotic-preserving continuum limit, rarefied-regime consistency, and regime-adaptive scaling of active kinetic degrees of freedom. Numerical tests in one, two, and three dimensions validate the accuracy, multiscale capability, and efficiency of the framework.

</details>

### [98] [Geometric bulk-edge correspondence for $\mathbb{Z}_2$-topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27318)
*Alexis Drouot,Jacob Shapiro,Xiaowen Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了二维时间反演不变绝缘体（Kitaev表中的AII类）在弯曲界面下的几何体边对应关系：当两个这样的绝缘体占据由弯曲边界分隔的互补区域时，界面系统的Z₂边缘指标等于两个体Z₂指标之差与边界及测量区域相关的几何交点数模2的乘积。这是对Hall绝缘体弯曲界面连接公式的Z₂类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过建立Z₂版本的弯曲界面连接公式，将体Z₂指标（Fu-Kane-Mele指标）与几何交点数（与边界和测量区域相关）关联起来，证明界面系统的Z₂边缘指标等于这两个量模2的乘积。

Result: 当两个时间反演不变绝缘体占据由弯曲边界分隔的互补区域时，界面系统的Z₂边缘指标等于体Z₂指标差与几何交点数模2的乘积。

Abstract: Fermionic time-reversal-invariant insulators in two dimensions--class AII in the Kitaev table--come in two topological phases. These phases are characterized by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-valued invariant, the Fu-Kane-Mele index. We prove a geometric bulk-edge correspondence for curved interfaces: if two such insulators occupy complementary regions separated by a curved boundary, then the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ edge index of the interface system is the product, modulo two, of the difference of the two bulk $\mathbb{Z}_2$ indices and a geometric intersection number associated with the boundary and the measurement region. The argument is a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ analogue of the curved-interface connection formula proved for Hall insulators in \cite{DZ24}.

</details>


### [99] [$\mathrm{W}^*$-algebraic Integration Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27366)
*Jan Głowacki,Yui Kuramochi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文定义了W*-代数值函数的POVM积分，建立了其泛函分析性质，包括积分域、W*-代数结构、映射的完全正性及算子值莱布尼茨规则与富比尼定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典测度论中的积分概念推广到非交换的算子代数框架下，建立基于POVM（正算子取值测度）的算子值积分理论。

Method: 利用空间张量积构造积分∫f⊗dE，通过超弱可测函数空间B_b和E-零函数商空间L^∞_E建立积分域，借助Stinespring分解和Naimark dilation证明完全正性。

Result: 积分映射是忠实正常单位完全正（CP）映射，对PVM是*-同态，对局部化POVM是等距；L^∞_E(Σ, M_S) ≅ M_S ⊗̄ L^∞_E(Σ)构成W*-代数；建立了算子值莱布尼茨规则和富比尼定理。

Conclusion: 建立了W*-代数框架下基于POVM的完备积分理论，统一了经典测度论与非交换概率论的积分概念。

Abstract: Given a pair of $\mathrm{W}^*$-algebras $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})$ with $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})_*$ separable, a measurable space $(Σ, \mathcal{F})$ and a POVM $\mathsf{E}: \mathcal{F} \to \mathcal{E}(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})$, the integral of a function $f: Σ\to \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}$ is defined as an element of the spatial tensor product $\int f \otimes d\mathsf{E} \in \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S} \bar{\otimes} \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R}$. The space $B_b(Σ,\mathcal{F},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})$ of uniformly bounded ultraweakly measurable functions is the universal domain of integration; once $\mathsf{E}$ is fixed it refines to the quotient $L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ,\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}) = B_b(Σ,\mathcal{F},\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S})/\mathcal{N}_\mathsf{E}$ by $\mathsf{E}$-null functions. When $(\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R})_*$ is also separable, $L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ,\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}) \cong \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S} \bar{\otimes} L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ)$ is a $\mathrm{W}^*$-algebra. The integration map is a faithful normal unital completely positive (CP) map, a $*$-homomorphism for PVMs and an isometry for localizable POVMs. It can be identified with the spatial tensor product $\boldsymbol{1}_{\mathcal{M}_\mathcal{S}} \hat{\otimes} Φ_\mathsf{E}$ where $Φ_\mathsf{E}: L^\infty_\mathsf{E}(Σ) \to \mathcal{M}_\mathcal{R}$ is the faithful normal positive map corresponding to $\mathsf{E}$. Complete positivity of integration maps is derived from Stinespring factorization through Naimark dilation. We establish an operator-valued Leibniz rule and Fubini theorem.

</details>

### [100] [Large-$N$ Carrollian Thermodynamics from AdS Black-Hole Phase-Space Contractions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26163)
*Yingnan Xu,Shuangshuang Chu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了有限卡罗尔黑洞热力学的边界与天球解释，通过双重缩放的低温大N系综实现了AdS第一定律的有限卡罗尔极限，并构建了相应的边界应力张量、热力学第一定律的边界形式以及天球基关联函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将AdS/CFT对偶中的黑洞热力学扩展到卡罗尔极限，解决有限条件下热力学量的发散问题，并赋予其全息与天球解释。

Method: 采用相空间压缩、双重缩放极限（低温大N）、布朗-亨诺中心荷归一化、布朗-约克应力张量构造以及傅里叶-梅林变换结合重标度热频窗方法。

Result: 得到了有限的第一定律线，识别了霍金-佩奇位置为自由度化学势零点，证明了有限第一定律是卡罗尔Ward恒等式的热零模扇区，构建了有限天球基关联函数。

Conclusion: 卡罗尔黑洞热力学具有一致的边界与天球全息解释，为理解极端时空中的全息原理提供了新框架。

Abstract: We develop the boundary and celestial interpretation of finite Carrollian black-hole thermodynamics. The bulk input is the phase-space contraction of the time generator and Newton constant for which the extended AdS first law has a finite Carrollian limit. We show that this finite first-law line has a holographic interpretation as a double-scaled low-temperature, large-$N$ ensemble: the Carrollian temperature decreases while the effective number of boundary degrees of freedom grows, leaving the thermodynamic products in the first law finite. The large-$N$ dictionary is anchored by the standard $\mathrm{AdS}_5/\mathrm{CFT}_4$ normalization of adjoint degrees of freedom and by the Brown--Henneaux central charge in $\mathrm{AdS}_3/\mathrm{CFT}_2$. We construct the finite Carrollian Brown--York stress tensor on the contracted AdS boundary and show that its global energy charge is the finite bulk Hamiltonian. We then derive the boundary form of the first law in terms of the spatial volume and the holographic degree-of-freedom normalization. This identifies the Hawking--Page locus with the zero of the chemical potential conjugate to the count of degrees of freedom. The same charge is the global Carrollian supertranslation charge, so the finite first law is the thermal zero-mode sector of the Carrollian Ward identity. Finally, we construct the celestial conformal-primary representation of thermal Carrollian correlators. The finite celestial-basis correlators are rescaled double-scaled correlators obtained by combining the Fourier--Mellin transform with the rescaled thermal frequency window.

### [101] [De Sitter Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26221)
*Kurt Hinterbichler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从物理学视角系统回顾了so(1,D)（D维德西特空间中所有等距代数）的表示，涵盖了所有维度D下的表示，包括混合对称表示和费米子表示，并将其与德西特空间上可以传播的各种场类型联系起来。

Method: 采用物理学家的视角，偏好具体构造而非抽象理论。系统梳理so(1,D)代数在各种维度下的表示，包括标量、矢量、张量（含混合对称性）以及旋量（费米子）表示，并将这些表示与德西特空间上实际传播的场类型一一对应。

Conclusion: 本文为德西特空间上的场论研究提供了统一的表示论框架，有助于推进德西特量子场论、宇宙学微扰论以及dS/CFT对偶等领域的研究。

Abstract: We review the representations of so(1,D), the algebra of isometries of D dimensional de Sitter space. We cover the representations in all D, including mixed symmetry representations and fermionic representations, and connect them to the various types of fields that can propagate on de Sitter space. The presentation is from a physics point of view, favoring concrete constructions over abstract considerations.

### [102] [Conserved charges and $L_\infty$ algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26224)
*Vinícius Bernardes,Theodore Erler,Atakan Hilmi Fırat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个在任意拉格朗日场论中计算守恒荷的公式，该公式完全基于理论的 $L_\infty$ 代数结构，无需依赖拉格朗日量的导数结构。这使得守恒荷可以在非局域模型（如弦场论）中计算，而传统方法在此类模型中失效。文章还展示了该公式正确表达了广义相对论中的表面荷（与Brown-York应力张量相关），并讨论了在杨-米尔斯理论中自然处理空间边界的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的守恒荷计算方法依赖于拉格朗日量的导数结构，这限制了其在非局域模型（如弦场论）中的应用。作者希望建立一个更普适的框架，仅利用 $L_\infty$ 代数结构即可计算守恒荷，从而推广到更广泛的场论模型中。

Method: 在 $L_\infty$ 代数框架下，推导出一个不依赖于拉格朗日量具体导数形式的守恒荷公式。通过将理论编码为 $L_\infty$ 数据，避免了传统方法中对局部导数结构的依赖，从而适用于非局域模型。

Result: 该公式在广义相对论中正确重现了表面荷，并与Brown-York应力张量一致；在杨-米尔斯理论中，空间边界问题也能被自然处理。这表明公式具有广泛的适用性和正确性。

Conclusion: 基于 $L_\infty$ 代数的守恒荷公式为拉格朗日场论提供了一种统一且普适的计算方法，尤其适用于非局域模型如弦场论。该工作为理解场论中的守恒量与边界条件提供了新的代数视角。

Abstract: We give a formula for conserved charges in an arbitrary Lagrangian field theory expressed in the framework of $L_\infty$ algebras. The formula is expressed in terms of the theory's $L_\infty$ data alone, without reference to the derivative structure of the Lagrangian. Therefore conserved charges can be computed in nonlocal models, such as string field theory, where conventional methods break down. We also show that the formula correctly expresses the surface charge of general relativity in terms of the Brown-York stress tensor. Related computations in Yang-Mills theory suggest that spatial boundaries are dealt with in a natural fashion.

### [103] [An observer's quantization of 3d de Sitter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26241)
*Andreas Blommaert,Damiano Tietto,Herman Verlinde*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出并计算了三维de Sitter静态斑的态密度，通过SL(2,ℤ)族的欧几里得无边界Kerr-lens时空（由线缺陷源驱动）来定义，并利用dS₃引力与复Liouville弦（ℂLS）⊗ ℂLS的全息对偶性进行精确量子计算，最终与半经典引力预言一致，为建立3d de Sitter的微观世界线全息图奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出通过SL(2,ℤ)族的欧几里得无边界Kerr-lens时空求和来定义态密度，这些时空由具有给定能量和自旋的线缺陷源产生（对应Lorentz时间中观察者在静态斑中心的世界线）。利用dS₃引力与两个复Liouville弦（ℂLS）拷贝之间的全息对偶，将Kerr-lens时空映射为SL(2,ℤ)族的广义crosscap几何，并计算ℂLS ⊗ ℂLS的crosscap振幅。对于最简单的非平凡Kerr-lens空间，进一步将其与双尺度SYK模型的GΣ有效场论联系起来。

Result: 计算得到的ℂLS ⊗ ℂLS crosscap振幅与半经典引力预言精确匹配。对于最简单的非平凡Kerr-lens空间，ℂLS ⊗ ℂLS描述进一步对偶于双尺度SYK模型的两个GΣ有效场论拷贝，该理论位于静态斑中观察者的世界线上。

Conclusion: 本文成功为3d de Sitter静态斑定义了态密度并实现了精确量子计算，结果与半经典引力一致，并建立了与SYK模型微观理论的联系，为构建3d de Sitter的微观世界线全息图铺平了道路。

Abstract: What is the density of states of the de Sitter static patch? We propose a definition and calculation of such a density in 3d dS. Our proposal involves a sum over an SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) set of Euclidean no-boundary Kerr-lens spacetimes sourced by a line-defect with given energy and spin - which in Lorentzian time represents an observer's worldline at the center of the dS static patch. We develop an exact quantum computation of the spectral density using a holographic duality between dS$_3$ gravity and two copies of $\mathbb{C}$LS, the complex Liouville string. The SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) Kerr-lens spacetimes map under the duality to an SL(2,$\mathbb{Z}$) family of generalized crosscap geometries. We compute the $\mathbb{C}$LS $\otimes$ $\mathbb{C}$LS crosscap amplitudes and show that they match the semi-classical gravity prediction. For the simplest non-trivial Kerr-lens space, the $\mathbb{C}$LS $\otimes$ $\mathbb{C}$LS description is, in turn, dual to two copies of the $GΣ$ effective field theory of the double scaled SYK model. The $GΣ\otimes GΣ$ theory lives on an observer's worldline in the static patch, setting the stage for developing a microscopic worldline hologram of 3d de Sitter.

### [104] [Charged and rotating near-horizon geometries in five dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26263)
*Alex Colling,Jun Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过解析方法构造带电荷和两个独立角动量的近地平几何解，并利用Sasakian结构证明在共转电场为非零常数的条件下，这些解是最一般的极端旋转视界。进一步将构造推广到高维Sasaki-Einstein流形。

Conclusion: 在无对称性假设下，这些解是共转电场为非零常数时最一般的旋转极端视界。高维Sasaki-Einstein流形可生成两参数族的带电荷自转视界。

Abstract: We present new charged and rotating near-horizon geometries in five-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell theory in closed analytic form. The solutions can be parametrised by the charge and two independent angular momenta. We also generalise these near-horizon geometries to theories with an additional Chern-Simons term in the action multiplied by an arbitrary coupling constant. The new solutions have the same entropy relations as expected for charged versions of extremal Myers-Perry black holes and for rotating versions of extremal Reissner-Nordström-Tangherlini black holes, but they do not reduce to the Myers-Perry horizon in the vacuum limit. The horizon cross-sections are spherical and carry a Sasakian structure. We exploit this structure to prove a characterisation of our solutions: without any symmetry assumptions, they are the most general rotating extremal horizons for which the co-rotating electric field is a (non-zero) constant. We further extend this construction to higher dimensions, where we show that any Sasaki-Einstein manifold generates a two-parameter family of charged and rotating horizons.

### [105] [Central charges $C_J$ and $C_T$ in QED$_d$-GNY model and scalar QED$_d$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26623)

The scaling dimensions of the lowest adjoint bilinear scalars are obtained to order $O(1/N)$ for general $d$. In $d=3$, the $U(1)$ Abelian gauge theory possesses a topological $U(1)$ global symmetry, and we evaluate the central charge $C_J^{\text{top}}$ of the topological symmetry current to subleading order in the $1/N$ expansion. Our interest in these theories is primarily motivated by their potential connection to the $SO(5)$ symmetric deconfined quantum critical point (DQCP). The large $N$ predictions of the QED$_3$-GNY model are found to be in reasonable agreement with the nonperturbative estimates for the $SO(5)$ DQCP.

### [106] [A Circle That Won't Return: The Fate of RR Fluxes and D-branes in Type 0A Tachyon Condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26280)
*Ahmed Rakin Kamal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究类型0A闭合弦快子与双倍Ramond-Ramond扇区，基于M理论在$S^1\vee S^1$（两圆在一点相接的楔形）上的描述。推导了快子驻点的分支平衡条件，分析了收缩分支RR数据在楔形塌缩至IIA端点时的命运，通过Gauss定律估计了长程RR场能成本，并描述了有效更高阶Stückelberg机制下的红外屏蔽，以及通过Wess-Zumino耦合识别的有效相对电荷载流子及其放电通道判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从类型0A运动方程出发推导分支平衡条件；使用Gauss定律估计长程RR场能；引入有效更高阶Stückelberg机制描述红外屏蔽；利用D膜的标准Wess-Zumino耦合识别相对电荷载流子并推导薄壁判据。

Result: 得到快子驻点的分支平衡条件；发现孤立未屏蔽的收缩分支$D_p^-$源的长程RR场能随收缩圆半径倒数发散；描述了相对RR场的红外屏蔽机制；导出了$D_p^- \to D_p^+$放电通道在参数化薄壁判据下可被能量优先的条件。

Conclusion: 类型0A中分支塌缩过程中RR数据不会消失而是通过Stückelberg机制被屏蔽，且存在通过相对电荷载流子实现的放电通道，其可行性由薄壁判据决定，这为理解快子凝聚与RR扇区耦合提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We study the closed-string tachyon and doubled Ramond-Ramond sector of type 0A in light of the proposed M-theory description on $S^1\vee S^1$-the wedge of two circles joined at a point. In this picture the two RR copies are associated with the two circle components, which we call branches, and tachyon condensation corresponds to shrinking one branch to the type IIA endpoint. From the type 0A equations of motion, we derive the branch-balance condition for a tachyon stationary point and identify the branch-odd RR fluctuation that sources the tachyon around a symmetric background. We then analyze the fate of the collapsing branch RR data as one branch of the wedge collapses to the type IIA endpoint. For an isolated unscreened collapsing-branch $D_p^-$ source, a Gauss-law estimate shows that the long-range RR field-energy cost scales inversely with the shrinking circle and thus becoming infinitely costly, generalizing the $D0^-$-brane decoupling in the original wedge picture. We describe the infrared screening of the relative RR field through an effective higher-form Stückelberg mechanism and distinguish this from a possible discharge of localized relative charge. Finally, using standard Wess-Zumino couplings of D-branes, we identify an effective relative-charge carrier and derive a parametric thin-wall criterion for when such a discharge channel $D_p^- \to D_p^+$ can be energetically favored.

The bulk geometry is constructed from exact black-brane solutions characterized by the fine-tuned Lovelock coupling $α$ and the highest power of curvature in the Lagrangian K. We then analyze the condensation of scalar and vector operators dual to minimally coupled matter fields, focusing on two bulk-field mass prescriptions, which significantly affect the superconducting phase. Our results demonstrate that higher curvature terms significantly modify the phase structure of both s-wave and p-wave systems and enhance the sensitivity of the condensates and critical temperatures to the gravitational couplings.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过参数化轨迹s^{α(t)}，其中α(0)=2-δ，分析不可约散射通道中的Shapiro/Wigner-Smith时间延迟。利用eikonal相位自然按t-通道不可约表示组织，而物理时间延迟是其s-通道本征值这一关键区别进行分析。

Result: 任何非单态轨迹当δ<1/2时会产生增长且符号不确定的时间延迟（δ=1/2为边缘情况，依赖于维度），这种延迟在弱引力机制下的Regge扩散区域占主导地位。非单态交换在物理通道中重新耦合时会产生正负两种符号，必然在至少一个通道中产生负的时间延迟。

Conclusion: 非单态交换必然导致某些散射通道中出现负时间延迟，这构成了对高能散射行为更严格的因果性约束，将等价原理的适用范围限制在单态交换情形。

Abstract: Recently, it was proposed that the leading high-energy behavior of scattering amplitudes is universal, independent of charge, thereby extending the equivalence principle beyond the graviton pole. In this Letter, we derive a sharper causality constraint on such behavior by studying the Regge limit of colored scattering. Parameterizing a trajectory by $s^{α(t)}$ with $α(0)=2-δ$, we analyze the Shapiro/Wigner--Smith time-delays in the irreducible scattering channels. We show that any non-singlet trajectory with $δ< 1/2$ produces a growing sign-indefinite time-delay (with $δ=1/2$ a marginal, dimension-dependent case), which becomes dominant in the Regge diffusion region in the weak-gravity regime. The essential point is that, while the eikonal phase is naturally organized in $t$-channel irreducible representations, the physical time-delays are its eigenvalues in the $s$-channel. A non-singlet exchange therefore recouples into the physical channels with both signs, inevitably producing a negative time-delay in at least one channel.

### [114] [Characteristic Lightcone Sources in SO(1,3) Yang-Mills Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27241)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者首先尝试对奇异分母进行实平移，发现这不能正则化源，反而将奇异支撑移至光锥外的双曲面，导致源无法同时保持守恒和无迹。进而提出在光锥上直接进行补全，通过匹配条件确定补全形式，该补全由一个参数χ决定。

Result: 实平移方案失败，因为位移后的支撑无法使源同时满足守恒和无迹；相比之下，光锥上的补全可以同时保持这两个性质。匹配条件将补全参数固定为χ，该参数具有因果解释——即未来锥与过去锥的相对权重。在正则的常时切片上，补全后的源总四动量为零，其物理内容表现为由曲率响应推断出的残余因果荷。

Abstract: The SO(1,3)-symmetric reduction of Yang-Mills theory on Minkowski space yields a stress-energy tensor that is smooth on the timelike and spacelike Lorentz orbits but diverges on the lightcone that separates the two regions. We ask what consistent source this singularity represents. A natural cure is a real shift of the singular denominator. This does not regularize the source but instead moves the singular support onto a hyperboloid off the cone, where the corresponding source cannot remain both conserved and traceless. Our analysis shows that the displaced support cannot retain both properties, whereas a completion on the lightcone can. The matching condition fixes this completion up to one parameter $χ$, which has a causal interpretation as the relative weight of the future and past cones. On regular constant-time slices, the completed source carries zero total four-momentum, so its physical content is a residual causal charge inferred from its curvature response.

Abstract: A remarkable universality appears in the low-temperature quantum thermodynamics of near-extremal black holes, where distinct parent geometries often lead to the same logarithmic temperature dependence at one loop. In this work, we study the Lichnerowicz spectral origin of this infrared universality and understand why the relevant spectral data become insensitive to the details of the parent geometry. For extremal near-horizon geometries containing a two-dimensional maximally symmetric throat, we construct the normalizable transverse-traceless tensor zero modes associated with near-horizon reparametrizations. Turning on a small temperature lifts these zero modes through the first-order deformation of the Lichnerowicz operator. Although the local matrix element depends on detailed parent-geometry data, these data cancel after projection onto normalized tensor modes, leaving the universal result. For static spherically symmetric backgrounds, the eigenvalue shift is universally proportional to the Fourier mode number and temperature, and the same structure persists for rotating backgrounds, where angular warp factors only modify the overall projection factor. We further show that this lifted bulk spectrum is the Lichnerowicz realization of the Schwarzian soft sector. Thus, the universal first-order result is traced to an infrared bulk-boundary matching between near-horizon tensor zero modes and boundary reparametrization dynamics.

*Nathan Belrhali,Arthur Poisson,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Laplace变换的通用方法，将宇宙学相关函数的弯曲时空模式分解为平面波叠加，从而将宇宙学费曼图转化为平坦时空对应图的积分表示。以单交换图为例，该方法以封闭级数形式解析计算，无需分段展开，揭示了能量奇点的结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学相关函数的计算通常依赖于特定的时空几何与动力学，现有方法在不同运动学区域需要分段展开，缺乏统一且计算高效的解析框架。

Method: 利用视界内每个宇宙学模式像平坦时空平面波一样振荡的事实，引入Laplace变换将弯曲时空模式分解为平面波叠加，核函数编码时空几何、场内容和动力学。由此建立图示化规则，将宇宙学相关函数图转化为平坦空间图在Laplace空间核上的积分。

Result: 对于典型的单交换图，该积分表示显式揭示了能量奇点，并以单一快速收敛级数的封闭形式在整个运动学域内计算，无需分段拼接不同的展开式。

Conclusion: Laplace方法为几乎所有早期宇宙理论中的宇宙学相关函数提供了概念和计算上的统一视角，简化了计算并揭示了深层结构。

Abstract: Deep inside the horizon, every cosmological mode oscillates as a flat-space plane wave. A Laplace transform turns this fact into a general method: it resolves each curved-space mode into a superposition of plane waves dressed by a kernel that encodes the spacetime geometry, field content and dynamics, collapsing the time integrals onto flat-space ones. This provides simple diagrammatic rules that turn cosmological correlator diagrams into their flat-space counterparts integrated against Laplace-space kernels. On the paradigmatic massive single exchange, this integral representation makes the energy singularities manifest and evaluates in closed form as a single, rapidly convergent series valid throughout the kinematic domain, with no patching of separate expansions. The Laplace approach sheds conceptual and computational light on cosmological correlators in virtually any theory of the early universe.

</details>


### [117] [Massive Cosmological Correlators from Flat Space: a Laplace-Space Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27311)
*Nathan Belrhali,Arthur Poisson,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的宇宙学关联函数计算方法在处理弯曲时空效应时计算复杂，作者希望利用哈勃半径内模式表现为平空间平面波的物理事实，发展一种更简洁、物理直观的计算框架。

Method: 利用拉普拉斯变换将弯曲时空中的模式函数分解为以对偶变量标记的平空间平面波的连续叠加，核函数编码时空几何、场内容和动力学信息。每个时间积分简化为基本的平空间积分，得到简单的图解规则。

Result: 以有质量单交换关联函数为例，拉普拉斯表示清晰地揭示了来自平空间的总能量和部分能量奇点，并给出了一个在整个运动学域内快速收敛的单一闭合级数解。

Conclusion: 该方法虽在德西特空间中共形耦合场与有质量标量场交换的背景下构建，但可几乎原封不动地推广到原始宇宙学中几乎所有感兴趣的情形，具有广泛的适用性。

Abstract: We develop a new approach to cosmological correlators, built on a simple physical fact: deep inside the Hubble radius every mode oscillates as a flat-space plane wave, the curvature of spacetime making itself felt only as the mode is stretched towards the horizon. A Laplace transform turns this observation into a computational tool, resolving each curved-space mode function into a continuous superposition of plane waves labelled by a dual variable and dressed by a kernel that encodes the spacetime geometry, field content and dynamics. Every time integral then reduces to an elementary flat-space one, yielding simple diagrammatic rules for cosmological correlators. We illustrate the construction on the massive single-exchange correlator. The Laplace representation makes its total- and partial-energy singularities transparent ''from flat space'', and yields a single closed-form, rapidly convergent series valid throughout the entire kinematic domain. Although developed for conformally coupled fields exchanging massive scalars in de Sitter, the approach carries over essentially unchanged to virtually all situations of interest in primordial cosmology.

</details>

Conclusion: 本文建立了D-instanton超引力解与IKKT矩阵模型之间的精确对应关系，为理解非共形p-膜的全息对偶提供了新视角，特别是BZJ流与超引力跑动之间的映射。

Abstract: Supergravity solutions describing stacks of D$p$-branes with $p\neq 3$ feature a non-constant dilaton profile, which is holographically mapped to the running of the SYM coupling in $(p+1)$ dimensions. For D-instantons ($p=-1$), the lack of space and time in the IKKT matrix model makes such an interpretation difficult at first. In this letter, we propose a method to achieve this based on two closely related concepts: the IKKT method of integrating out heavy strings in a Coulomb branch vacuum and the matrix RG flow of Brézin and Zinn-Justin (BZJ). The notable difference between the two is that the BZJ RG flow also integrates over the Coulomb branch position. We first apply the Coulomb branch method and by relating the coefficient of the leading correction to the IKKT action with the string coupling, we can compute its dependence on the Coulomb branch position, finding a match between matrix theory and supergravity. Next, we apply the BZJ-flow to the IKKT partition function, which leads to a running of the coupling constant $g$ with the rank $N$ of the matrix model, reproducing the $N$-dependence of the axio-dilaton field in supergravity.

### [120] [Approximating Feynman integrals using complete monotonicity and Stieltjes properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27101)
*Sara Ditsch,Johannes M. Henn,Prashanth Raman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出两种基于完全单调性和Stieltjes性质数值计算Feynman积分的新方法：CM bootstrap方法利用微分方程重构积分无需边界条件，Stieltjes函数方法利用Padé逼近实现快速解析延拓与数值计算，并以20-loop banana积分等实例验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用Feynman积分在Euclidean区域的完全单调性（所有导数符号固定）这一普适解析性质，发展无需边界数据即可重构积分、并能提供严格界限的新数值方法，同时进一步证明其在特定参数范围内具有更强的Stieltjes函数性质，从而利用Padé逼近实现高效解析延拓与数值计算。

Method: 1. CM bootstrap：基于Feynman积分在Euclidean区域的完全单调性，从微分方程出发重构积分，无需显式边界数据，可给出严格界限。2. Stieltjes函数方法：证明Feynman积分在特定参数范围内不仅是完全单调的，更是Stieltjes函数，进而利用具有可证收敛性的Padé逼近，在带割线的复平面上实现解析延拓与快速数值计算。

Result: 以massive bubble积分为简单实例验证了方法有效性，并将方法推广至多圈积分，包括20-loop banana积分等高阶情形。两种方法均能实现Feynman积分数值计算。

Conclusion: 基于完全单调性和Stieltjes性质的两种新方法为Feynman积分数值计算开辟了新途径，具有无需边界条件、提供严格界限、可证收敛等优势，并可推广至更广泛的Feynman积分计算场景。

Abstract: We present two novel approaches for the numerical evaluation of Feynman integrals based on their universal analytic properties related to positivity, namely complete monotonicity (CM) and Stieltjes properties. Building on recent results, we exploit the fact that scalar Feynman integrals in the Euclidean region are completely monotonic functions, meaning that all their derivatives have a fixed sign. Building on this observation, the CM bootstrap allows one to reconstruct integrals from differential equations without explicit boundary data, yielding rigorous bounds. The second method is based on a refinement of CM. We prove that Feynman integrals, within a certain range of parameters, are not only CM but in fact Stieltjes functions. This enables the use of Padé approximants with provable convergence properties in the cut complex plane, providing an efficient method for analytic continuation and fast numerical evaluation. We illustrate the method with simple examples such as the massive bubble integral and discuss applications to multi-loop integrals, including the 20-loop banana integral. Finally, we comment on a number of extensions of these novel avenues for computing Feynman integrals.

</details>


### [121] [Probing Probability Geometry with Schwinger--Dyson Identities: Score Mismatch, Fisher Information, and Configurational Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27360)
*Anosh Joseph*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了Schwinger-Dyson恒等式的几何解释，指出其违背由一个单一的得分失配场 δs = ∇log(Q/P_eq) 控制，该场刻画了与平衡态的偏离。相对Fisher信息是其模平方，由此导出了Fisher信息与完整Schwinger-Dyson层级之间的普适界，并给出了相对Fisher信息的变分刻画，建立了层析成像解释。构型温度作为特殊的Schwinger-Dyson探针出现，Stein算子和得分函数方法自然源于同一概率几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Schwinger-Dyson恒等式提供一个统一的几何框架，揭示其违背的根源，并建立与Fisher信息、构型温度、非平衡采样等概念之间的内在联系。

Method: 引入得分失配场 δs = ∇ log(Q/P_eq)，将每个Schwinger-Dyson恒等式解释为该场在构型空间中探针方向上的投影；利用相对Fisher信息作为该场的模平方，推导普适界；给出相对Fisher信息基于Schwinger-Dyson违背的变分刻画。

Result: 所有Schwinger-Dyson违背均由单一得分失配场决定；Fisher信息收敛可恢复所有Schwinger-Dyson恒等式；相对Fisher信息可由Schwinger-Dyson违背变分刻画；构型温度作为特殊探针出现；Stein算子与得分函数方法自然融入同一几何框架。

Conclusion: 得分失配场为理解Schwinger-Dyson恒等式、构型温度、Fisher信息及随机过程中的非平衡采样提供了统一的几何语言。

Abstract: We develop a geometric interpretation of Schwinger--Dyson identities by showing that their violations are controlled by a single score-mismatch field $δs$. For an arbitrary sampled probability distribution $Q$ and equilibrium measure $P_{\rm eq}$, every Schwinger--Dyson violation is determined by $δs = \nabla \log (Q / P_{\rm eq})$, which characterizes the departure from equilibrium. Each Schwinger--Dyson identity measures a projection of this field onto a probe direction in configuration space. The relative Fisher information is its squared norm. This gives a universal bound relating Fisher information to the complete Schwinger--Dyson hierarchy, thus implying that convergence in Fisher information restores all Schwinger--Dyson identities. We further obtain a variational characterization of the relative Fisher information in terms of Schwinger--Dyson violations, leading to a natural tomographic interpretation in which increasingly rich families of probe fields encode progressively more information about the underlying probability distortion. The configurational temperature, within this framework, emerges as a distinguished Schwinger--Dyson probe. The Stein operators and score-function methods arise naturally from the same probability-geometric structure. The score-mismatch field, therefore, provides a unified geometric language for understanding Schwinger--Dyson identities, configurational temperature, Fisher information, and non-equilibrium sampling in stochastic processes.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典Poisson代数的形变量子化问题推广到顶点算子代数的手征版本，建立顶点Poisson代数的形变量子化理论框架。

Method: 运用operadic方法，构建顶点Poisson代数的形变量子化的逐阶形变-障碍理论，该理论由手征Poisson上同调控制。

Result: 建立了顶点Poisson代数形变量子化的形变-障碍理论；对于仿射辛流形弧空间上的函数顶点Poisson代数，证明了该理论由de Rham上同调控制；证明了边界Virasoro极小模型在形变下是刚性的。

Conclusion: 成功建立了顶点Poisson代数的形变量子化的operadic框架，并在仿射辛流形和边界Virasoro极小模型两个重要情形中得到了具体应用。

Abstract: We give an operadic approach to deformation quantization of vertex Poisson algebras, a chiral analogue of the traditional problem of deformation quantization of Poisson algebras. Our main result is an order-by-order deformation-obstruction theory for such quantizations, controlled by the chiral analogue of Poisson cohomology. In the special case of chiral quantizations of affine symplectic varieties, quantizations of the vertex Poisson algebras of functions on their arc spaces, we prove that this deformation-obstruction theory is controlled by their de Rham cohomology. As another application, we prove that the boundary Virasoro minimal models are rigid under deformations.

</details>


### [127] [Coquasi-bialgebroids and cocycle twisting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27343)
*Xiao Han,Shahn Majid*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文引入非交换基代数上的coquasi-bialgebroid概念，利用Takeuchi的×B-余代数形式，要求余积保持代数映射到Takeuchi积，而乘积仅在可逆归一化3-上链意义下结合。发展了基本理论并证明了卷积可逆2-上链的扭结定理，构造了coquasi Connes-Moscovici型bialgebroid，并在有限投射性假设下描述了其对偶拟bialgebroid构造及其与Drinfeld型扭结的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在非交换基代数上建立coquasi-bialgebra的bialgebroid类比，为cocycle扭曲的bialgebroid构造提供自然框架。

Method: 采用Takeuchi的×B-余代数形式，要求余积为代数映射到Takeuchi积，乘积由可逆归一化3-上链控制结合性；通过卷积可逆2-上链进行扭结；在B⊗H⊗B上构造示例；在有限投射性下建立对偶构造。

Result: 建立了coquasi-bialgebroid的基本理论，证明了扭结定理，构造了以coquasi-bialgebra H测量代数B为输入的Connes-Moscovici型例子，给出了有限群例子（子群G⊆X及横截选择），描述了对偶拟bialgebroid及其与Drinfeld扭结的关系。

Conclusion: coquasi-bialgebroid是coquasi-bialgebra在非交换基代数上的推广，为cocycle扭曲构造提供了统一框架，且与对偶拟bialgebroid和Drinfeld型扭结有密切联系。

Abstract: We introduce coquasi-bialgebroids over a noncommutative base algebra. Using Takeuchi's \(\times_B\)-coalgebra formalism, we require the coproduct to remain an algebra map into the Takeuchi product, while the product is associative only up to an invertible normalized \(3\)-cocycle. This gives a bialgebroid analogue of coquasi-bialgebras and provides a natural framework for cocycle-twisted bialgebroid constructions.
  We develop the basic theory and prove a twisting theorem by convolution-invertible \(2\)-cochains. As a main class of examples, we construct coquasi Connes--Moscovici-type bialgebroids on \(B\otimes H\otimes B\), where \(H\) is a coquasi-bialgebra measuring an algebra \(B\), with twisting data \(γ:H\otimes H\to B\). We also give finite-group examples arising from a subgroup \(G\subseteq X\) and a choice of transversal. Finally, under finite projectivity assumptions, we describe the dual quasi-bialgebroid construction and its relation to Drinfeld-type twisting.

</details>
